regnum britanie nunc di tur anglia may ye see englonde fyrste began albyon albyon pafore wyll speke brute shall shewed londe englonde fyrst named albion encheson named noble londe si ie ryall kynge myghty man grete renomee called dyoclesyan well worthely hym gouerned ruled thrugh noble chyualry conquered londes hym almoost kynges worlde hym attendaunt pit befell thus dyoclesyan spowsed gentyll damoysell wonder fayre emys doughter labana loued hy reason wolde gate vpon xxxiij doughters whiche eldest called albine damoysels whan came vnto aege became soo fayre wonder wherof dyoclesyan anone lete make sompnynge comaunded letter kynges helde hym sholde come certayne daye letter conteyned make feest ryall whiche daye thyther came brought admyralles prynces duke noble chyualry feest ryally arayed lyued ioye myrthe ynough wonder wyte befell thus dyoclesyan thought marye doughters amonge tho kynges solempnyte pand spake dyde albine eldest doughter systers rychely maryed vnto xxxiij kynges lordes grete honour power solempnyte whan solempnyte done euery kynge toke wyf ladde ther owne countree de quenes pand befell thus afterwarde dame albene became stoute sterne tolde lytyll pryce lorde hym scorne despyte wolde wyll wolde haue owne wyll dyuers mater systers euerychone bare soo euyll ayenst ther lordes wonder wyte moche thought ther husbondes hyghe parentage come ther fader kinges ther lordes wold haue chastysed fayre manere vpon loue frendshyp sholde amende ther selfwylled codycyons al nought dyde ther owne wyll thynge lyked power wherfore xxxiii ky ge vpon tyme oft tyme bete ther wyues wende wolde amende theyr tatches ther wyckednesse suche condycyons fayre speche warnynge dyde wors betynges eftsones moche wors wherfore kynge wedded albyne wrote tatches condycyons hsi wyfe albine lettre sente dyoclesyan fader whan kyges de albines lorde sent letter dioclesian anone sente letter sealed ther seales condycyons tatches ther wyues whan kynge dioclesian sawe herde many playntes doughters sore ashamyd became wonder angrye wrothe towarde doughters thou ghte thenne myghte amende mysdyde anone sente letter vnto xxxiii kynges sholde come hym brynge wt theym theyr wyues euery chone att certeyne daye wolde chastyse theym theyr wyckednesse yf myghte ony manere wyse soo kynges came atte tyme daye tho sette betwene hym kinges dyoclesyan resceyued theym moche honoure made solempne feest vnderneth lordshyp thyrde daye solempnyte kynge dyoclesyan sente xxxiij doughters sholde come speke hym chambre whan come spake ther wyckednesse ther cruelte spyteuously repreued blamed sayd yf wolde chastysed sholde loue lese euer whan ladyes herde became abasshed gretely ashamed ther fader sayd wolde make ndes departed ther faders chambre dame albine eldest syster ladde theym chambre tho made voyde therin persone amonge systers gyder ptho sayd albine fayr systers well knowe kyng fader v hath reproued shamed dispysed cause make v obedyent vnto husbondes certes shall neuer whyles lyue syth come hygher kyng blode myn husbonde whan thus sayd systers sayd tho sayd albine well wote fayre systers husbondes haue complayned vnto fader vpon v wherfore hath v thus foule reproued dispysed wherfore systers cousell nyght whan husbondes ben bedde one assente kytte ther throtes thenne may pea better mow thynge vnder faders power ouer elles anone ladyes consented graunted counsell whan nyght comen lordes ladyes wente bedde anone ther lordes slepe kytte theyr husbondes throtes slewe whan dyoclesyan theyr fader herde thynge became furyously wrothe agaynst doughters anone wolde haue brente baron lordes sirrie counseyled suche streytnesse owne doughters oonly sholde voyde londe euer neuer sholde come ayen dyde dyoclesyan ther fader anone comauded go shyppe delyuerd vytaylles half whan done systers wente shyppe saylled forth see betoke ther frendes apolin ther god longe saylled see tyll last came arryued wyldernesse whan albion come londe systers albine wente fr ste forth shyppe sayd systers moche sayd eldest syster company fyrst londe hath taken moche myn name alb londe called alb myn owne name anoue sters graunted good tho wente systers pe tooke londe albron ster called wente downe founde neyther men man ne childe wylde beest uerse kyndes whan dyspended fayled de herbes season yere lyued best myght toke flesshe dyuerse beestes became wonder fatte desyred mannes company mannes kynde fayled bere wered wonder courageous kynde desyred mannes company ony solace myrthe whan deuyll perceyued wen e dyuerse countrees toke body ay lykynge nature shad men came londe albion laye tho wymen shadde tho nature vpon conceyued brought forth gyautes whiche one called gogmagog longherigam named dyuers name maner came forth borne horryble gyautes albion dwelled caues hylles ther wyll londe albion lyked vnto tyme brute arryued came totnes yle albion brute conquered scomfyted gyauntes aboue sayd pexplicit prima par phere begynneth brute goten slewe fyrst moder fader conquered albion named brytayne owne name callid englonde name engyst sa onte pthis brute came brytayne xviij yere hely knowen noble cyte grete troy noble knyght man grete power called eneas whan cyte troy loste destroyed thorugh grece eneas meyne fledde then came lombardy tho lorde gouernour londe kynge called latyne kyng called turocelyne strongely warred vpon kyng latyne oftentymes dyde hym moche harme whan kynge latyne herde eneas come receyued hym moche honour hym helde moche herde hym wyst well noble knyght worthy body dedes eneas helped kynge latyne warre shortely telle well worthely dyde slewe turocelyne dyscomfyted hym people whan done kynge latyne gaaf londe turocelynes noble man eneas maryage wt lauyne doughter moost fayrest creature ony man wyst lyued togyder ioye myrthe dayes ther lyf tyme pand ascanius sone eneas wedded wyf vpon gate sone called silueyne silueyne whan coude reason man vnwetynge fader ayenst wyll aqueynted hym damoysell cosyn lauyne kynge latynes doughter quene eneas wyf brought damoysell childe whan ascanius fader wyst anone lete enquyre wysest maysters grettest clerkes childe damoysell sholde brynge forth answered sayd sholde brynge forthe sone sholde kylle bothe fader also moder dy de moder deyed berynge hym whan childe borne fader lete calle hym brute maysters sayd sholde moche harme sorowe many dyuers place sholde come greate honour worshyp kyng ascanius deyed whan god wolde silueyne sone receyued londe made hym wonderly well beloued amonge people whan brute silueynes sone xv yere olde wente vpon daye fader playe solace brute sholde haue shot vnto herte arowe myshapped glaced brute slewe fader phow brute dryuen londe helde hym grece whan myschaslce befall people londe made sorowe ynough sore angred encheson therof droue brute londe wolde suffre hym amonge whan sawe myght abyde wente then grece founde vij thousande men lygnage kynrede troy come grete blood story telleth men wymmen childern whiche holde thral dome bondage kynge pandras grece dethe achilles betrayed slayne troy brute wonder fayre man stronge huge aege gladde chere semblaunt also worthy body wel beloued amonge people kynge pandras herde speke goodnes condicyons anone made hym dwelle hym soo brute became wonder preuy mo che beloued kynge longe tyme brute dwelled kynge last troy brute spake togyders kynrede lygnage acquayntaunce playned vnto brute ther sorowe ther bondage many shame kynge pandras done vnto brute sayd vpon tyme ye lorde lygnage stronge man myghty ye capytayne lorde gouernour wyll become men comaundementes maner thynges brynge v wretchednesse bondage wyll fyghte kynge trouthe grace grete god shall hym ouercome shall make kynge londe homage shall holde euer brute tho grete py te theyr bondage brought pryuely wente theym kynges courte tho troy went put woodes mountaynes helde sente vnto kynge pandras sholde gyue leue sauely wende londe wolde noo lenger dwelle bondage kynge pandras wexed tho sore anoyed tho swore sholde slee euerychone ordeyned grete power wente towarde fyght brute men manly defended fyersly fought slewe kynges men none escaped toke kynge helde hym person ordeyned cousell bytwene myght done sayd sholde put deth sholde exiled londe sayd sholde te tho spake wyse yght called mempris sayd te tho troy yf kynge dras wolde yelde hym haue lyf counseyll gyue vnto brute duke souerayne doughter gennogen wyf hondred shyppes well de tresoure golde come wyne mocke nede haue thynge thenne go londe ordeyne v londe elles ne none kynrede come v shall neuer haue pea londe amonge theym grece haue slayne soo many ther u ghtes frendes euermore wa contake sholde amonge v brute tho folke consented well counseyll thynge tolde kynge pandras haue lyf graunted moche axed anone gaf vnto brute gennogen doughter wyf bondred shyppes wt asmoche neded vytaylles afore ordeyned brute tho toke wyf men forsoke londe grece went vnto see wynde weder ther wyll came thyrde daye ile called lorgres brute anone sente men londe espye maner cou tree foude olde cyte wasted forlet na therin nother man ne woman ne thynge dwellynge myddell cyte founde olde temple fayre lady yt called dyana goddesse came ayen vnto brute tolde hym seen founde counselled hym go sacrefyce vnto dame dyana wonte yeue answere thynge euer men prayed namely vnto honoured sacrefyce brute wente vnto ymage sayd dyana noble goddesse thynge noble wherin ye shall alwaye honoured whan done prayer dyana answered maner brute sayd go euen forth thy waye ouer see fraunce towarde west ye shall fynde yle called albyon yle becompassed wt see man moche strongest men droue scomfyted feblest toke ther londes yt euery countree grete warre stryf vnder amonge thynges amonge coutree yt ouercame yt thrugh ther myght strengthe toke londes euery toke kynge cornewayle cloten sholde haue londe reason cause man wyst none ryght heyre strongest lette lytell lesse estate therfore cloten londe amonge cornewaylle pof kynge donebant clotens sone wanne londe cloten sone called donebant deth fader became hardy man fayr curteys passed kynges fayrenesse worthynesse anone knyght wyst well yt whan fader lyued moost ryghtful heyre londe sholde haue reason kynges moche strenghte toke hym londe afterwarde donebant ordened hym grete power conquered fyrst londe loegers wolde haue conquered londe scotlonde walys scater came men yaue hym batayll rudac came southwarde brother brenne lond humber vnto scotlonde pbut moche yt belin better parte brenne therfore wexed wroth wolde haue londe belin brother wolde graunte hym wherfore cotake warre arose amonge taken pthe kynge olsynges lete assemble grete hoste delyuered doughter brenne people assembled damoysell samie longe tyme loued kynge called gutlagh hym tolde counsell yt brenne sholde haue lede hym euer sholde lese myght forsake brene whan gutlagh herde tydynges lay aspye brenne many shyppes myght haue soo two fletes mette togyder longe tyme faught soo brennes men tourned ayen dyscomfyted kynge gutlagh toke samie put shyppe brenne shamefully fledde then man dyscomfyted kynge gutlagh wolde haue gone owne coutree came vpon hym suche grete tempest fyue dayes lasted thorugh tempest dryuen brytayne thre shyppes moo tho kepte costes see toke gutlagh samie folke presented belin belin put pryson phow belin droue londe ky ge gutlach denmark samie longe yt brenne came agayne grete nauy sente brother belin sholde yelde ayen londe wyse folke castelles also elles wolde destroye londe pbelin dradde noo thynge malyce wolde thynge hadde sayd wherfore brenne came folke fought belin brenne dyscomfyted folke slayne hymself fledde xij men fraunce belin brennes brother wente thenne yorke toke counseyll sholde kynge gutlagh kynge gutlagh profered become man holde londe hym yeldynge yerely mli syluer euermore surenesse couenaut kep e gutlagh sholde brynge hy good hostage hy sholde homage folke yet sholde swere vpon boke yt sholde neuer broke ne fayled belin tho couseyll folke grauted hym arynge gutlagh became man belin vndertoke hym homage othe wrytynge ye couenautes vpon couenautes kynge gutlagh toke samie folke went then torned ayen denmark euer couenauntes holden treuage payed gynder kymbalyns sone wolde paye truage rome londe cassybolon graunted slayne romayne deth kymbalyn regned gynder sone good man worthy hygh herte wolde pay rome trybute kynge cassybolon grau ted vnto iulius cezar wherfore perour tho called claudius cezar sore anoyed ordeyned grete power romayns came londe conquere trybute thrugh strength haue kynge kynge gynder arinager broder assembled grete hoste brotons yaue batayll emperour clawdius slewe romayns grete plente emperour afterwarde one called hamon sawe people fast slayne pryuely cast awaye owne armes toke armes deed bryton armed hym armour came bataylle kyuge sayd maner syr good herte goddes loue romayns ben enmyes anone shall slayne dyscomfyted euerychone kynge gaaf kepe wordes ne speche cause armes vpon hym de myd ben bryton traytour euer helde hym next kynge pryuely vnder sholder armes smote kynge wherfore kynge deyed felle downe erthe p whan armager sawe brother deed caste awaye armes toke hym brother armes came batayll amonges brytons hadde hetfly fyght fastlaye downe romayns armes wende kyng gynder afore slayne wyst thenne began brytons fyersly fyght slewe romayns laste emperour forsoke felde fledde fast myght folke wynchestre fals traytour hamon slayne kynge fast anone beganne slee al hast myght armager kynges brother pursued hym full fyersely fyers herte droue hym vnto water toke hym anone smote bothe honde foot heed ed body pyeces thenne lete cast hym water wherfore water called hamons hauen made fayre towne yet stondeth called southampton armager wente wynchestre seke claudius cezar emperour rome armager hym toke claudius themperour thorugh counseyll romayns wt hym lefte lyue made pea armager maner ye shal saye claudius emperour sholde yeue vnto armager gennen fayre doughter haue vnto wyf soo londe tyme forwarde sholde emperours power rome vpon suche couenaunt neuer afterwarde emperour rome sholde take none trybute londe oonly frauce accorded vpon couenaunt claudius cezar sente rome antioche apostle dyuers coutrees armager regned well worthely gouerned londe ryght worshypfully pand claudius cezar remembraunce accorde reuerence honoure doughter made londe fayre towne castell lete openly apostle dyuerse londes ryght fayth pand whan armager hadde regned xxiiij yere deyed lyeth auncyente cyte london phow kynge westmer gaf berynger ylonde forlet berynger made towne berwyke armager regned sone westmer good man worthy body well gouerned londe befell yt tydynges came hym vpon daye kynge roderyk gascoyne come londe hughe hoste people dwellynge stanys whan kynge westmer herde tydynges lete assemble huge hoste brytons came kynge roderyk yaue hym batayll kynge westmer slewe kynge roderyk owne hondes playne bataylle whan kynge roderyks men sawe ther lorde slayne yelded kynge westmer became men euer gaf coutree forleten wherin myght dwelle thyther wente dwelled theyr lyues tyme ix hondred men theym moo lefte batayll theyr gouernour prynce called berynger anone began towne myght therin dwelle haue resorte lete calle towne berwyk vpon twede enhabyted became ryche wymen amonge brytons wolde yeue theyr doughters straugers wherfore wente ouer see irlonde brought wymen spowsed men coude vnderstonde theyr langage ne speche wymen therfore spake togyder scottes afterwarde thrugh chaugynge ther langage frauce called thenne scottes soo sholde folkes countree called euer phow kynge westmer lete arere stone entrynge westmerlonde slewe roderyk began fyrst housynge batayll aboue sayd whan roderyk deed kynge westmer remembrauce victory lete arere besyde waye grete stone hygh yet stondeth euer shall stonde le te graue stone letter yt thus sayd kynge westmer brytayne slewe place roderyk enemye p westmer fyrst buylded hous towne westmerlonde stone begynneth westmerlonde haue kynge whiche noble knyght stronge man called conan meriedok sholde haue kepte kynges doughter haue maryed whan tyme ben lordes londe wolde suffre yaaf couseyll maryed hyghe man grete honour maximian became ryall thought conquere londe armorycam grete rychesse yt herde telle yt londe ne lefte man yt worthynes knyght squyre ne none man ne toke hym grete damage londe lefte home behynde hym man kepe londe toke hy fro londe xxx thousande knyghtes doughty mennes bodyes wente ouer londe armorycam slewe kynge called imball conquered londe whan done called conan sayd moche kyng octauian made moche brytayne soo shall men knowe one brytaytayne fro conan meridok thanked hym greetly made kynge lytell brytayn whan done maximiam wente then vnto rome tho made emperour constantyne conan dwelled lete come afore hym london lete ordeyne shyppes hastely moche neded vyage toke owne doughter called vrsula fayrest creature ony man wyst wolde haue sent kynge conan sholde haue spoused made quene londe made pryuely god vowe chastyte fader wyst ne none man elles lyuynge vpon erthe phow vrsula xi thousande maydens company wente towarde lytell brytayne martred coleyne vrsula chose vnto company xi thousande maydens lady maystresse wente shyppe one tyme water called tamyse comaunded kynne frendes almyghty god saylled towarde lytell brytayn whan come hyghe see stronge tempest arose goddes wyll vrsula shyppes company dryue hundlonde thrugh tempest arryued hauen cyte coleyne kyng londe called gowan tho cyte whan wyst tydynges ny fayre maydens arryued toke elga brother housholde hym went shyppes se fayre company whan sawe fayre company wolde haue ouerlayne sake fro ther maydenhode vrsula good mayde couseylled prayed warned taught theym felowes sholde defende theyr myght rather suffre deth suffre ther body defor led tho maydens became stedfast god defended thrugh grace none hadde power shame wherfore kynge gowan sore ano ed wrathe slewe eueryone anone ryght tho maydens martred loue god lyeth coleyne phow kynge gowan came destroy londe man grete power called gracian deffended londe done kynge gowan sarrasyn called brother elga sayd hym sholde goo conquere londe fayr maydens borne ordened tho grete power pehites denmarke orkenay norway came londe brente townes slewe folke cast downe chirches house robbed londe length brede put deth tho wolde forsake ryght byleue crystendome moche souerayne myght helpe kynge maximian take hym worthy men whan wente conquere lytell brytayne tyme ye telle saynt albon martryd thrugh wood tyraut dyoclesian place abbaye made saynt albon whyles paynym conuerted hy god thrugh predicacon clerke wyse man called ancyble herbourghed nyght hous thyncarnacyon ihesu cryst ij hondred xxvi yere men shall vnderstonde saynt albon suffred martyrdom saynt edmonde martryd therfore saynt albon called fyrst martyr englond pthis gowans brother folke sarrasyns wente thrugh londe destroyed thynge fou de thynge spared whan tydynges came rome kynge gowan begon destroye londe emperour rome sente stronge man grete power called gracian xxiiijm well fyghtynge men caste sarrasyns londe arryued portesmouth pmaximian myght come hyself moche chosen emperour deth constantyne saynt eleynes sone whan gracian arryued wt hoste lete aspye pryucly kynge gowan myght founde sette vpon sodenly laye theyr beddes dyscomfyted hym slewe ther beddes euerychone none scaped sauf gowan fledde owne coutree wt moche sorowe grete payne pso oneafter befelle maximian slayne rome thrugh treason whan gracian wyst tydynges lete crowne hym kynge londe phow gracian made hy kynge whan maximian slayne afterwarde brytons slewe hy wyckednesse gracian whan began regne became wycked sterne moche sorowe dyde brytons slewe hy amonge ptho whan kynge gowan vnderstode gracian slayne done deth assembled grete power came ayen londe yf fyrst done harme tho dyde moche tho destroyed londe crysten people moche brytayne man hardy name god dyde anone put strange deth pbut bysshop london tho called gosselim scaped went then rome seke socour helpe destroy sarrasyns destroyed londe romayns sayd ben often enoyed ther sendynge people brytayne helpe brytons wolde nomore bysshop gosselin went then without ony secour helpe tho wente kynge lytell brytayne called aldroye thyrde kynge gowan meryedok sayd pthe bysshop prayed aldroye helpe socoure kynge pyte herte whan herde bysshop fledde crysten men soo slayne grete brytayne thrugh paynyms sarrasyns grauted hym constantyn broder hym helpe power folke dyde arraye hors armour shyppes thynges neded vyage whan thynge redy called bysshop hym sayd take constantyne broder vpon couenaut yf god gyue hym grace paynems sarrasyns destroye ye make hym kynge bysshop grauted wt good wyll pconstantyne bysshop toke leue kynge aldroye betoke hym god toke ther men xij thousande wente ther shyppes saylled towarde grete brytayne arryued att totnesse pwhan brytons herde tydyng came socour strongely holpen ordeyned anhuge nombre people came receyued moche honour pgowan anone wyst tydynges assembled sarrasyns came ayenst yaue batayle constantyne slewe hy owne hondes sarrasyns dyscomfyted slayne none escaped conuerted vnto almyghty god phow constantyne yt kynges brother lytell brytayne crowned kynge grete brytayune grete vertue grete worthynesse anone batayll wente london crowned constantyne made hym kyng londe bysshop gosselyn sette crowne heed anoynted hym befalleth kynge tho began crystendome ayen londe anone kynge constantyne crowned anone spowsid wyf thrugh couseyll brytons begate thre sone fyrste called constance aurilambros thyrde vter constance elder brother whan ca aege made hym monke att wyncestre constantyne ther fad er thrugh treason slayne pfor befell tyme pehite came hy vpon daye message sayd wolde speke foe kyng pryuely couseyll kyng lete voyde chambre men within abode noo moo kynge pehite made cou tenaunce though wolde haue spoken kynge eere slewe hym longe knyf went meruaylously chambre chamre laste man wyst become pwhan kynges men west theyr lorde deed made moche sorowe wyst moche two sone aurilambros vter yonge myght kynge thyrde monke sayd vortiger erle westsex thought pryuely herte thrugh queyntaunce kyng hym selfe wente wynchestre constance monke sayd vnto hym constance sayd fader deed two brethern ben gosselyn bysshopp london nourysshe yonge none may bynge wherfore cousell ye forsake habyte come shall make suche meane vnto brytons ye shall made kynge pof constance kynge constantynes sone monke atte wynchestre made kynge faders dethe thorugh counseyll vortiger erle westsex moche aurilambros vter two brethern yonge aege vortiger lete slee hym kynge hymself vortiger couselled constance moche tyll forsoke abbot wente hym anone crowned kynge thassent brytons kynge constance whan crowned made kynge wyst ne knewe lytell worlde ne coude nothyng knyghthode axed made vortiger chyef mayster couseyller gaaf hym power ordeyne moche reame aperteyned hymself nothynge entremedled oonly bare name kynge whan vortiger sawe londe warde gouernall thought preuy treason slee constance kynge myght hymself crowned made kynge regne lete sende hondred knyghtes pehites worthyest londe helde hym dwelle kepers body wolde go thorugh londe ordeyne thynges apperteyned kyng vortiger honoured moche hondred knyghtes moche yaue golde syluer ryche iewelles robe horse thynges plentee wherfore helde hy lorde dyd kyng vortiger tolde yf myght ky ge ye thrugh treason wolde make rychest londe soo last thrugh grete gyftes gyuen largely cryed thrugh courte vortiger better worthy kyng constance wherfore vortiger made semblaunt hadde ben wroth departed then court sayd must go elles thynges hadde traytour sayd cause sholde slee hym saye constance pwhad vortiger gone befell soone tho hondred knyghtes pehites brake doores kynges chambre hym slewe smote heed bare vortiger dwelled whan vortiger sawe heed wepte full tenderly eyen neuertheles somdeale gladde herte deth pand anone vortiger toke hondred knyghtes pehites badde seruauntes bynde theyr hondes behynde ladde london dampned vnto deth fals traytours anone brytons londe comyn assente crowned vortiger made hym cronycles englonde shall sette togyder tyll shall treate alured whose tyme dane came englonde pope emperours kynges tyme shall sette togyder pcirca annu dm cccc xlix phow wardeyns childern kepe constantynes ladde theym lytell brytayne treason falsenesse vortiger tyme came saxon pagan fyrst brytayne called englonde vnder vortiger whiche crowned kynge londe pthis tyme two childern kepynge constantynes sone saye aurilambros vter thrugh ordynance gosselin bysshop london faders deth saye constantyne durste dwelle londe childern conueyed vnto kynge lytell brytayn moche tho wyst treason vortiger tho made kynge thorugh whome constance elder brother slayne wherfore hondred knyght pehites put deth bore blame vortiger wyst therof ne consented kepers two childern dradde lest vortiger sholde put deth thrugh treason falsenesse done brother therfore ladde ouer lytell brytayn kyng receyued moche honour lete nourysshe dwelled tyll became fay knyght stronge fyers thought auenged vpon constance theyr brother whan sawe theyr tyme soo dyde ye shall telle afterwarde pit longe afterwarde tydynges came ouer see kynrede hondred knyght pehite dampned put deth thrugh vortiger londe therfore wonderly wrothe swore wolde auenged theyr kynnes men deth came londe grete power robbed many place slewe dyde sorowe myght whan vortiger wyst made moche sorowe sore anoyed place also tydynges came hym aurtlambros vter brother assembled grete hoste come moche brytayne say londe auenged vpon constance theyr brother deth soo one half brought soo moche sorowe ne wyst whether go phow engist xi thousande men came londe whome vortiger yaa e place called thongcastell soone sorowe tydynges came vortiger grete nauy straungers arryued coutree kent wyst whens ne wherfore come londe pthe kyng sent anone messager thyder sholde come speke hym wyte folke axed countree wolde p two brethern maysters prynces stronge company one called engist yt horne engist wente kynge tolde hym cause wherfore come londe sayd syr ben cou tre yt called saxonie londe germayne wherin moche sorowe people ben many londe may susteyne maysters prynces haue londe gouerne rule made come men wymmen boldest ben amonge theym fyght best may trauayll dyuerse londes sholde yeue horse harneys armour thynge nedeth shall saye go another countree mowe lyue theyr auncetrees dyde therfore syr kynge yf ye haue ought company ben comen londe good wyll wolde serue londe kepe helpe defende enmyes yf ye nede pwhan vortiger herde tydynges sayd gladly wolde theym withholde vppon suche couenaunt yf myght delyuer londe enmyes wolde yeue theym resonable londes sholde dwelle euer pengist thanked hym goodly maner company xi thousande sholde dwelle kynge vortiger moche dyde thrugh theyr boldenesse delyuered londe enmyes clene ptho prayed engist kynge moche londe myght make hy cyte meyne pthe kynge answered without counseyll brytons pengist prayed hym eftsones moche place myght compace wt thonge skynne wherupon myghte make maneer hym dwelle kynge hy graunted freely ptho toke engist bulles skynne kytte smale myght thonge rounde therwith compaced moche londe myght thenne make vpon fayre castell whan castell made lete shyppes fylled men stronge also well fyghtynge bataylles sholde also brynge ronowen doughter fayrest creature man myght see pand whan people come sente toke castell moche ioye hymself vpon daye wente vnto kynge prayed hym worthely wolde come see newe maneer made place compassed thonge skynne pthe kynge anone grauted hym freely hym wente thyder well apayed castell fayre werke togyder ete dranke theyr lorde souerayne couseyler euery batayll crowned hym made hym kynge wolde suffre vortiger lenger regne cause alyauce betwixt engist hym pthe brytons ordeyned grete hoste dryue engist company londe yaue hym thre bataylles fyrst kente lorde seconde te orde thyrde shyre half colchestre batayle theym mette catagien home engistes brother eche theym slewe moche cou tree yeuen longe horne thrugh vortiger tho spowsed cosyn made fayre castell called horncastell owne name vortimer soo anoyed brother deth anone lete fell downe castell groude ne lefte nyght ne daye tyll dryuen engist people londe kynge engist came londe fought togyders vortimers deth brytonr theyr comyn assente eft soones made vortiger theyr kyng vpon couenaut sholdde neuer suffre engist ne none eft sone come londe whan done best whan wyse men longe tyme studyed sayd kyng sholde seke childe borne woman neuer man childe sholde slayne tempre blood morter werke soo sholde werke euer endure withouten ende phow kynge lete seke merlyn thorugh walys speke wt hym kynge herde co maunded messagers anone go thrugh walys seke childe yf myght hym fynde sholde hym brynge forth vnto hym recorde wytnesse kynge take letter ne wyse men abasshed coude answere merlyn tho sayd kynge syr shall tell cause wherfore werke thus fayleth may stande vnder mountayne ye haue buylded toure grete ponde water botome ponde vnder water ben two dragon one whyte reede fyght togyder ayenst werke ye myne depe tyll men come ponde cause men take awaye water thenne ye shall see dragon haue tollde togyder fyght ayenst werke cause wherfore suche poyson slepe anone ryght deyed slepynge traytour sayd wolde go felde tyll awaked escaped awaye man hym suspeccyon cause habyte clothed also brode shauen crowne whan kynges men wyst deed became castall tyntagyll pand kynge lete ordeyne grete hoste came cornewaylle destroye erle yf myght put hym suche castell stronge well arayed called tyntagyll wolde yelde hym kynge pand kynge anone besyeged kynge vter syke myght helpe hy self ordeyned aloth sone eleyne tho chosen wardeyne chyeftayne folke anone brytons assembled grete hoste yaue batayll octa folke octa last dyscomfyted pit befell thus afterwarde brytons dedignacon aloth wolde hym attendaue wherfore kynge anoyed wonder sore lete put hym lytere hoste amonges folke ladde hym vereloyne tho fayre cyte saynt albon martred cyte destroyed paynems thrugh warre thyther sente octa os ther people entered towne lete make sure yates helde kynge came besyeged made stronge assawee within manly theym deffended p kynge lete ordeyne ginnes engynes breke walles walles stronge man myght mysdo pocta people grete despyte kynge lyenge lytere theym besyeged toke counseyll amonge stande vp morowe erly come yeue batayll kynge dyde batayll bothe octa os slayne escaped lyue fledde scotlnde made colegrin theyr chyeftayne saxon lyue escaped fro batayll brought ayen grete strength amonge sayd yf kynge vter deed spolde well conquere londe thought enpoysen kynge ordeyned men dede yaue yeft grete plente thynge ordeyned thyderwarde kynge dwellynge clothed poore wede better spede theyr fals purpose netheles theyr falsenes subtylte myght neuer come nygh kynge last aspyed kynge dranke lycour oonly water clere well nyghe besyde fals traytours vpon daye pryuely wente well put therin poyson water enpoysened anone kynge dronke water began swelle soone deyed many dranke water deyed also anone aspyed folke towne lete stoppe welle euermore pwhan kynge deed folke bare hym stonhenge grete solempnyte bysshop baron hym burye besyde aurilambros brother torned ayen tho euerychone sente sone made hym kynge londe moche reuerence faders de xvij yere regne phow kyng arthur sone vter crowned fad deth draue colegrin sarons cheldr k almayne londe arthur made kynge londe yonge aege xv yere fayre bolde doughty body meke folke good curteys large spendynge made hym well beloued amonge nede whan began regne swore truely saxon neuer sholde haue ne pea tyll hadde dryurn londe assembled greate hoste fought colegrin whiche tyme octa deed saxon mayntened colegrin dyscomfyted fledde vnto yorke toke towne hym helde kynge besyeged hy myght thynge spede cyte stronge within towne kept cyte well orpedly pand mene tyme colegrin lete towne bladulf fledde hymself cheldrik kynge almayne haue hym socour kynge assembled grete power came arryued scotlonde xv hondred shyppes whan arthur wyst tydynges power strength ynoughe fyght ayenst cheldrik lete syege wente london sente anone letter kynge lytell brytayne yt called howell neuewe systers sone sholde come hym wt power yt myght assembled grete hoste arryued southampton kyng arthur wyst gladde ynough wente ayenst receyued wt moche honour two host mette assembled toke theyr waye euen vnto nicholl cheldrik besyeged taken came vpon cheldrik people wyst egrely assaylled pthe kyng cheldrik men defended hym manly theyr power kynge arthur men slewe many saxon neuer seen suche slaughter cheldrik men left alyue fledde awaye kynge arthur pursewed droue wood myght ferder passe pchildrik men sawe well brought moche dysease yelded kynge arthur maner wyse sholde take theyr horse theyr armour muste oonly goo foot theyr shyppes wolde go home theyr owne londe neuer come ayen londe pand vpon assuraunce thynge hy good hostage pand arthur counseyll men grauted thynge receyued hostage therupon wente theyr shyppes whan hygh see wynde chau ged deuyll wolde forned theyr nauy came ayen londe arryued totnesse wente shyppes toke londe dene robbed moche people slewe tooke armour myght fynde wente forth tyll came vnto bathe men towne shytte faste theyr yates wolde suffre theym come within towne deffended well orpedly ayenst phow arthur yaue bataylle vnto saxon whan came agayne londe besyeged towne bathe ouercame anone arthur herde tydynges lete hange hostage lefte howell brytayne neuewe kepe marche towarde scotlonde half people hym self wente helpe rescowe towne bathe whan came thyther yaue stronge batayll cheldrik slewe almoost people man myght hym withstonde ne endure vnder ye stroke swerde bothe slayne colegrin bladult brother cheldrik fledde then wolde haue gone shyppes pbut whan arthur wyst toke x thousande knyghtes cador erle cornewaylle lette stoppe mynge arthur hymself wente towarde marche scotlonde mesengers tolde hym scottes besyeged howell brytayne laye syke horne berde syluer shall come nosethryll dompe shall betoken hungre sorowe grete deth ye people moche londe begynnynge regne shall wasted pthis gote shall go ouer vnto frauce shall open ye floure lyf batayll shall called whyte batayll forsayd beer shall gote moche harme shall come southwest blood thenne shall gote lese moche londe tyll tyme shenshyp shal hym ouercome shall close hym lyon skynne thenne shall wynne loste therto people shall come north west shall make gote sore aferde shal grete perplexite shall aduenge hym enmyes thrugh cou seyll two owles fyrst shall peryll vndone olde owle shall wende waye certayne tyme shall come ayen longe two owles shall grete harme many one shall couseyll gote arere warre ayenst forsayd beer laste gote owles shall come burton vppon trent shall go ouer drede beer shall flee swanne hym fro company burton warde north shall wt harde shoure thenne shall swanne take slayne sorowe beer taken heeded alther next neest shall stande vpon broken brydge whome lonne shall cast beemes many shall hym seke vertue hym shall come pin shall deye sorowe care peple londe londes shall vpon hym bolder afterwarde two owles shall moche sorowe forsayd floure lyf became lyege men tooke homage pand kyng arthur torned ayen hoste came vnto yorke made bydynge durynge vyage tho gaue logrys aloth spowsed syster gyftes grete plente tho gawyn cosyn yonge aege men hym whan wyst arthur came ordeyned hoste grete power fought kynge folke dyscomfyted fled vnto parys entred cyte closed yates helde pwhan arthur wyst froll gone parys pursued came thyder hym besyeged cyte hungre came vnto froll prayed hym accorded kynge arthur haue pea wolde yelde theym vnto hym cyte also pfroll sawe myght lenger holde towne ayenst theyr wyll trusted gretly vppon owne strength sente sholde fyght anone smote togyders fyersly well fought bothe sydes man demed better befell froll yaue arthur suche stroke kneled grounde wolde nolde froll wouded kynge arthur forhede blood fell downe destroye crysten men god shall v helpe ouercome haue ryght opynyon therfore haue truste god enmyes crystendome god may destroyed ouercome men may recorde warthynesse knyghthode pwhan kyng arthur hadde yf soth wyll haue vnto wyf pthis knyght called edelwolde went forth waye kynge hym sayd came lady whan sawe fayre thought haue hymself wyf therof spake orgarus fader fader olde man moo childern oonly roode london stretes couered ouer heed sylke tapyser ryche couerynges ioye comynge burgeys cyte caste att theyr wyndowes golde syluer hondes full tokenynge loue worshyp seruyce reuerence condyte chepe ranne whyte wyne reed stremes doth water euery man dranke therof wolde theyr owne wyl kyng edwarde crowned enoynted ryght heyre englonde moche honour masse kyng wente place holde ryall feest amonge dyde hym honour whan sette meete kynge alexander scotlonde came hym honour reuerence queyntesye hondred knyghtes hym well horsyd arayde whan alyght theyr stedes lete theym goo whether wolde myght take toke theyr owne wyll without ony chalenge came syr edmond kynge edwardes brother curteys knyght gentyll renowne erle cornewaylle erle glocestre thenne came erle penbroke erle garenne eche themself ladde theyr honde hondred knyghtes gayly dysguysed theyr armes whan alyghted theyr horse lete go whether wolde myght catche haue styll withoute ony chalenge whan alle done kyng edwarde dyde dylygence myght amende dresse wronges beste manere myght honour god holy chirche mayntene honour amende noyaunce comyn people phow ydeyne lewelyns doughter walys prynce aymer erles brother mounforde taken see fyrste yere warde kynge edward crowned lewelyn prynce wale sente fraunce erle mountforde thorough cou seyll frendes erle sholde wedde doughter erle tho auysed hy vpon thynge sente vnto lewelny sayd wolde sende hys doughter sent aymer broder damoysell lewelyn arayed shyppes doughter syr aymer fayre company sholde goo lewelyn dyd grete wronge couenauted sholde yeue doughter noo manere man without counsell consent kynge edwarde befel burgeys brystow came see wyne laden mette toke myght power anone burgeys sente theym ky ge whan lewelyn herde tydy ge wrothe also sorow full gan warre vpon kynge edwarde dyd moche harme vnto englysshmen bete downe kynges castels began dystroye kyng edwardes londe whan tydynges came vnto kynge thynge wente walys somoche dydd thoroughe goddes grace greate power drofe lewelyn vnto grete myscheyf fledde maner strenth came yelded hym vnto kynge edwarde yaue hym l marke syluer haue pea toke damoysel herytage made oblygacio kynge edwarde come parlemente two tymes yere seconde yere kynge edwarde crowned helde generall parlement westmestre made statute defaute lawe comune assente baronage atte ester nexte sewenge kynge sente letter vnto lewelyn prynce wale sholde come parlemente londe holdynge wale strenthe letter oblygatory wytnessyd tho lewelyn scorne dyspyte kynges commaundement pure wrathe ayen began werre vpon kynge edwarde dystroyed londes tho whanne kynge edward herd thyse tydynges wexed wonder wrothe vnto lewelyn hast assembled people wente hym toward wale warred vpon lewelyn prynce tylle broughte hym moche sorowe dysease lewelyn sawe defence myghte hym notte auaylle came ayen yelded hym kynges grace hym mercye longe tyme kneled kynges fote kynge hym pyte commaunded hym aryse mekenes foryaue wrathe hym sayd yf trespassed hym nother tyme wold dystroye hym euermore pdauyd lewelyns broder tyme dwelled kynge edwarde felle man subtyll enuyous also ferre castynge moche treason thoughte euermore made good semblaunt semed true man myght perceyue falines phow lewelyn thrugh eggynge brother dauyd werryd agayn vpon kyge edwarde longe tyme kynge edwarde yaf dauyd lewelyus broder lordshyppe frodesham made hym knyght moche honour dyd neuer walys bycause hym kynge edward helde parlement atte london whan hadde walys wolde chaunged money full yll kytte wherfore people playned sore kynge enquered tres passours iii hudred atteynted suche maner falsnes wherfore hanged drawe hangyd afterwarde kynge ordeyned sterlynge halfpeny ferthynge sholde go londe commaunded man fro daye afterwarde yaue ne feoffedhous relegyon londe tenement without specyall leue kynge dyde sholde punysshed kynges wyll yefte shall noughte longe lewelyn prynce wale thrugh tycemet dauyd brother bothe theyr consent thought dysheryte kyng edward asmoche myghte thorough bothe kynges pea broken whan kynge edwarde herde anone sent hys baron northumberlonde surrey also sholde go take theyr vyage vpon traytours lewelyn dauyd wonder herd warte tho wynter walys whan countres somer lewelyn lete ordeyne well araye vytayll good castell swa therin huge nombre people plente vytaylles kynge edward wyst entre whan kynges men perceyued also strenthe walys lete come see bargee botes grete plankys many myght ordeyne haue go sayd castel swandon men fote alsoo hors walsshmen moch people stronge draue englysshmen ayen ther somoche presse people tornynge ayen charge burden men made barge botes synke drowned many good knyghte saye syr robert clyfford syr wyllyam lyndeseye syr iohns sone fitz robert syr rycharde tanny huge nobre thrughe ther owne foly yf gode espyes harmyd wha kynge edwarde herde tell people drowned made sorowe inoughe tho came syr iohn vessy fro kynge arago brought hym moche people bachelers gascoynes souldyours dwelled wt sayd iohn vessy receyued hym wage hym witholde noble men fyght brente many townes slewe moche people walsshmen myght take tho strenthe myght made assawte vnto castell swa gate castell whan da uyd prynce brother herde tydynges ordeyned hym flyght lewelyn prynce saw broder fledde sore abasshedde hadde power warte mayntene lewelyn gan flee wende welle haue scapedde morowe syr roger mortymer mette hym oonly wt x knyghtes sette hym rounde aboute hym went smote heed presentyd heed vnto kynge edwarde manere lewelyn pry ce walys taken hede smyten also heyres dysheryted euermore thrugh ryghtfull dome lordes reame phow dauyd lewelyns broder prynce walys putte dethe dauyd prynces broder walys thrughe pryde wende haue prynce walys hys brother dethe vppon sente walsshemen parlement dynbygh folysshely made walys aryse ayenste kynge began meue werre ayenste kynge edward dyd sorowe dysease myght power whanne kynge edwarde e thinge ordeyned men pursewe vpon hym dauyd fyersly hym defended tylle came towne saynt morice dauyd take fledde ladde kynge kynge commauded sholde hangyd draw en smyte heed quarter hym send hede london four quarter sende four chyef townes walys sholde take ensample therof beware afterwarde kyng edwarde lete crye pea thrugh oute wale seased londe honde grete lordes lefte alyue came feautee homage kynge edwarde theyr kynde lorde tho lete kynge edwarde amende lawes walys defectyue sent lordes walys letter patentes sholde come al parlemente whan come kynge sayd full curteysly lordynges ye welcome behouethe couseyll helpe go gascoyne amende trespasse done whan entreate pea bytwene kynge aragon prynce morrey ky ge lyege men erles baron consented graunted therto tho made hym kynge ed warderedy went galcoyne lete amende trespass hym doon ingascoyne debate bytwene kynge aragon prynce morrey sessed made theym accorded whyle good kynge edwarde elynore wyfe gascoyne gode erle cornewayll made wardeyn englonde tyll kynge edwarde came ayen tho enquered traitours coniected falsnesse agaynste hym eche receyued therdome deserued meane tyme good kynge edwarde beyonde see doo make amendes ayenste hym trespassyd ther false yf traytoure called rysapp merydok bega make werre ayenste kynge edward cause syr payne tiptot wrongfully greued dyseased forsayd rysap merydok whan kynge edwarde herde matere well vnderstode none sente letter pryue seale forsayd rebellyon rysap merydok sholde begynne manere wyse make reyse werre sholde pea loue whan came ayen englonde wolde vnder take quarell amende mysdon forsayd rysap mer dok dyspysed kynges comaudement spared doo sorowe myght kynges men englonde anone take ladde yorke drawen hangyd felonye pof dressynge kynge edward made iusti clerkes doon ther falsnes draue iewes englonde ther vsury myshyle e kynge edwarde hadde dwelled thre yere gascoyne desire came hym goo englonde ayen whanne come aye founde many playntes made hy iustyces clerkes hadde done many wronges falsnesse wonder whiche falsnesse syr thomas waylond kynges iustice forswore englonde toure london falsnesse men put vpon hym wherfore atteynt proued fals anone whan kynge done wyll iustices tho lete enquere espye iewes dysceyned begyled people thorough synne falsnesse vsury lete ordeyne preuy parlement amonge lordes deyned amonge theym iewes sholde voyde englonde theyr mysbyleue also theyr fals vsurye dyd vnto crysten men spede make ende thynge comynalte englonde yaue vnto kynge xv peny theyr goodes meuable soo iewes dryuen englonde tho went iewes fraunce dwellyd thrugh leue kynge phylyp tho kynge fraunce phow kynge edwarde seased londe scotlonde thrugh consente graut lordes scotlode longe alex andre kynge scotlond dede dauyd erle huntyngdon kynges brother scotlo de axyd claymed kyngdom scotlonde hys brother deed cause ryghtfulle heyre many grete lordes sayd nay wherfore greate debate arose bytwene theym ther fredes asmoche wolde consente coronacyon meane tyme forsayd dauyd deyed befell sayd dauyd thre doughters worthyly maryed fyrste doughter maryed bailol seconde brus thyrde hastynges forsayd baylol brus chalenged londe scotlonde grete debate stryf arose bytwene cause eche wolde haue kynge whan lordes scotlonde saw debate bytwene came ky ge edwarde englonde seased hy lond scotlonde chyef lord whan kynge seased forsayd lordes forsayd baylol brus hastynges came kynges courte axyd kynge whiche sholde kynge scotlonde kynge edwarde full gentyll true lete enquere cronycles scotlonde grettest lordes scotlonde whiche eldest blood founde baylol eldest kynge scotlonde sholde holde kynge englonde hym feaute homa ge done bailol te scotlonde crowned kynge scotlonde pand time vpon see grete warre bytwe ne englysshmen norman vpon tyme norman arryued douer martred holy man called thomas douer afterward norman slayne escaped one pand afterwarde kynge edwarde sholde lese duchye gascoyne thrugh kynge philyp frauce thrughe fals castynge dousepers londe wherfore syr edmonde kynge edwardis brother yaue vp homage vnto kynge fraunce pand tyme clerkes englond graunted kynge edwarde halfe deale holy chirche goodes helpynge recouer londe agayne gascoyne kynge sent thethere noble company bachelers hymself wolde haue gone po tesmon let thrugh one maddok walys hadde seased castell swandon honde cause kynge tomed walys crist masse bycause noble lord englonde sent gascoyne hadde comforth ther lorde kynge take syr charlys fraunce say syr iohn brytayne syr roberte tiptot syr rau e tanny syr hughe bardolfe syr adam cretynge yet ascensyon maddok take walys nother called morgan sent tour londo byheded phow syr iohn baylol kynge scotlonde sayd homage whan syr iohn baylol ky ge scotlond vnderstode kynge edwarde werred gascoyne whome ye reame scotlonde delyuerd falsly tho ayenst oth wt sayd homage thrugh procurynge folke sent vnto ye courte rome thrugh fals suggestyon assoylled ye othe yt swore vnto ye kynge englode letter enbulled ptho chose scotlonde dousepers benyme edwarde hys ryght pand yt tyme came two cardynalles ye courte rome fro celestine trete acorde bytwene kynge fraunce kynge englonde tho cardynalles spake acorde thomas turbeluyll taken lyos made homage warde parys putt sone hostage thought go englonde aspye ye countre tell whan came englonde broken kynges pryson fraunce nyght sayd yt wolde englysshmen walsshmen sholde abowte kynge frauce thyng brynge ende swore vpon couenaut dedes made bytwene yt sholde haue yere thousand poundes worth londe brynge thynge ende fals traytour toke leue wente then came intoo englonde vnto kynge sayd yt broke pryson yt put hym suche peryll loue wherfor kyng cowde hym moche thanke full gladde comynge pand fals traytoure fro daye aspyed doynge kynge also counselle kynge loued hym full well hym full preuy clerke englonde yt kynges hous fraunce herde treason falsnesse wrote another clerke yt tho dwellynge wt edward kynge englonde thomas turbeluyll done fals coniectynge counsell englo de wryte haue sende vnto kynge frauce thrugh ye forsayd letter yt clerke sente fro frauce foude vpon hym wherfor led london hangyd drawe treason two sone put fraunce hostage thenne beheeded pof conquest berwyke whan twoo cardynalles gone agayne fraunce trete pea cambroy kynge sent thether erles baron saye syr edmonde broder erle lancastre lecetre syr henry lacy erle nicholl wyllya vessy baron baronettes abowte xiii best wysest englonde pand tyme ky ge edwarde toke vyage scotlonde vpon iohn baylol kynge scotlonde pand syr robert roos berewyk fledde fro englyshmen wente scottes ky ge edwarde wente hym towarde barwyk besegyd towne thoo within manly defended sette fyre brente two kynge edwarde shyppes sayd dyspyte repreyf hym wenyth kynge edwarde longe shankys haue gete berewyk vnthankes gas pykes hym whan doon gas dyke hym whan kynge edwarde herde scorne anone thrugh myghtynesse passed ouer dyches assaylled towne came ya e gate conquered towne thrughe gratyous power slewe xxv thousad vij hondred scottes ky ge edward lost man renoune sauffyr rychard cornewayle hym kylled flemynge redde halle wt quarell forsayde rycharde dyd helme commaunded theym yelde put ky ge grace scottes wolde notte wherfore halle brent caste downe tho therin brent kynge edwarde lost moo men vyage symple estate xxvii englysshmen wardeyn castell yaue vp keyes castel wythout ony assawte taken syr wyllyam douglas symond frysell erle patryk yeldyd pea ingham humlresmylle robert brus yt wyth kynge edwarde forsoke kynge edwarde helde scottes afterwarde taken put pryso thoo lete kynge edwarde close berewyk walles dyches robert rous went tyndale set wuyerbrydge fyre exham lamerstok slew robbyd ye folke coutre yt went fro then dunbatre fyrst wenesdaye marche kynge sent erle garenne syr hugh percy syre hughe spenser fayre company besege castell one called syr rycharde sywarde traytoure fals man ymagyned begyle englysshemen sente englysshmen theym desceyue sayd wolde yelde theym castell yf wolde graunte viii dayes respyte myght sende telle syr iohan baylol kynge scotlonde howe men fared within castell pand sende hym worde yf wolde remene sege englysshe men wolde yelde castell vntoo englysshe men pthe messenger thoo came syr iohn baylol thoo kynge scotlonde hooste messengre told hym alle caas syre iohn toke hoste came morowe erly towarde castell syr rycharde sywarde sawe hym come mayster counsell keper castell sayd vntoo englysshmen osayd nowe ise fayre company well appareylled woll go ayenste theym mete theym assaylle syr hugh spenser sawe falsnesse hym treason sayde hym traytour take proue falsnesse shall auaylle hughe spencer comaunded anone bynde hym hast went ayenst ther enmyes slewe scottes xxii thou sande scottes tyme noo man wyth honour sauf patryk graham manly foughte longe last slayne thoo sayd englysshmen repreyf scottes thyse scaterande scottes holde scottes wrench vnware erly mornynge euyll tymynge wente ye fro dunbare pa tho ware within castell sawe scomfyture yelded vp castell vnto englysshemen bounde theyr bodyes godes castels kynge edwarde take castell thre erles vii baron xxxviii knyghtes xi clerkes vii pycardys presentyd kynge edwarde sent towre londo kept phowe kynge edwarde greate grace delyuerede ayen scottes oute pryson cheyftayns londe drew frensshemen thrugh couseyll wyllyam waleys kynge edwarde made tho ende werre take cheyfteyns scotlonde thoo came syr iohn baylol yelded hym vnto ky ge edwarde put hym grace ledde london whan kynge edwarde come thether brought hym kynge axyd wolde make amendes trespaas losse hadde doon hym put heym mercy lordynges sayd kynge wyll londes ne goodes wyll ye make othe vpon goddys body true te neuer tyme ayenst bere army consentyd kynges wyll swore vpon goddys body saye syr iohn comyn erle strathorn erle carryk also four bysshops vndertoke clergye kynge delyuerd yaue sauf conduyt go ther owne londe longe afterward nearyse aye kynge edwarde cause wyste well kynge edwarde folke take gsacoyne sayd syr iohn baylol kynge scotlonde wyst well londe sholde haue sorow shame theyr falsnesse haste went hym ouer see owne londes helde hym came neuer aye wherfore scottes chose vnto theyre kynge wyllyam waleys rybaude harlot comen vp nought moche harme dyd englysshmen kynge edward thought myght haue delyueraunce people take gascoyne hast went hy ouer flaundres werre vppon kynge fraunce erle flaundres receyued hym moch honoure grautyd hym alle londys owne wyll whan kynge frauce herde tell kynge englo de aryued flaundres came grete power hym dystroye prayed hym trewto two yere englysshe marchauntes also frenche myghte saufly go come bothe sydes kyng edward geaunted muste haue men pryson gascoyne kynge frauce anone grauted delyuerd pand tyme scottes sent bysshop saynt andrewes fraunce kynge syr charles brother syr charles sholde come power scotlonde wolde come theyr power sholde go englonde londe dystroye scotlonde vnto came kent scottes trustyd moche vpon frensshmen thynge manere graunte netheles scottes began robbe kylle northuberlonde dydd moche harme phow wyllyam waleys lete reyse londe scotlonde cheyf lorde syr hughe cressynham bataylle fonkyrke tydynges come kyng edward wylliam waleys ordeyned suche stronge power also scotlonde hym attendaunt redy lee englyssh e dystoye londe sore anoyed sente anone letter therle garienne syr henry perry wyllyam latomer syer hughe cressynham cresorer sholde take power go northumber londe forth scotlonde kepe coutrees whan wyllyam waleys herde theyr comyge began flee englysshmen hym folowed drout hym tyll came ryu lyn helde hym castell walsshmen euery daye escryed menacyd dyd dyspyer myght soo englysshemen vpon tyme mornynge wente oute fro castell moutenaunce x mile passed ouer brydge wyllyam waleys came stronge power droue theym abak englysshmen ayenst hym power tho fledde myght take brydge scaped syr hugh kynges tresorer slayne many also wherfore made moche sorowe ptho kynge edward sped mater flaundres come ayen englonde hast toke way scotlonde came thederat ascencyon tyde foude sette fyre brent poore people scotlonde came hym wonder thyck prayed hym goddys loue wolde haue mercy pyte wherfore tho kynge comaunded man sholde harme yolden hym ne man ordrene hous relygyon ne manere chirche lete espye myght wher myght fynde ony enmyes tho came spye vnto kynge tolde scottes assembled abyde bataylle saynt mary mawdeleyns daye kynge came fonkyrk yaue bataylle scottes batayle slayn xxx thousande scottes englysshemen xviii mo whiche worthy knyght slayne knyght hospytylere callyd frery brian iay whan wyllyam waleys fledde batayll frery brian hym pursewed fiers ly hors ranne stert myre mary vp bely wyllyam waleys torned tho agayne slewe forsayd brian moche harme pand whyle kynge edwarde wente thorough scotlonde enquere yf myght fynde ony enmyes londe dwelled longe hym lyked enmye durst hym abyde pand soone kynge edwarde wente southampton wolde abyde scotlonde wynter season esement people whan came london lete amende many mysdedys done ayenst pea lawes beynge flaudres pof laste maryage kynge edwarde wente thyrde tyme scotlonde ordeyned thrughe court rome kynge edwarde sholde wedde dame margarete kynge phylip syster frau ce archebysshop robert wy chelse spousyd togyders thrugh whiche maryage made pea bytwene kynge edwarde englonde kynge philyp frauce pkyng edwarde went tho thyrde tyme scotlond tho within fyrst yfre enfamyned londe left one ne came mercye sauf castell estreuelyn well vytaylled stored vii yere phow castell estreuelyn seged wonne bynge edwarde came castell estreuelyn wt huge power besegyd castell lytyll auaylled myght scottes none harme castell stronge well kept kynge edwarde sawe bethought hym vpon queyntesy lett make anone two payr hygh galowes tour castell made othe many within castell notwithstandynge erle baron take strength yf wolde rather hym yelde sholde hangyd vppon galowes whan tho within castell herde came yelde kynges grace mercy kynge foryaa male talent grete lordes scotlonde swore kynge edwarde shold come london euery parlemet sholde stonde ordynaunce phow troylebasto fyrst ordened kynge edwarde went then london wende haue reste pea warre whiche werre occupyed xx yere saye gascoyne walys scotlonde thought myght recouer tresour spended abowte werre lete enquere thrugh reame tyme hadde reame men called troillebaston ordeyned therto iustices manere recouered tresour without nombre purpose haue goon holy londe haue werred vppon goddes enmyes cause crossyd longe tyme netheles law ordeyned dyd moche good thrugh englonde myshode thoo trespassed well chastysed meke better poore comyns reste pea tyme kynge edwarde prysoned owne sone edwarde cause walter lanton bysshop chestre ky ge tresorer complayned hym sayd forsayd edwarde thrugh cousell entysynge one ganaston squyre gascoyne broke park forsayd bysshop pers couselyd lad edwarde cause ky ge exyled sone englonde pof dethe wyllyam waleys fals traytoure whan kynge edward hadde enemyes ouercome walys gascoyne scotlonde dystroyed traytours rybaude wyllyam waleys neuer kynge wolde hym yelde att towne saynt domynyk yere kynge edward regne xxxiii fals traytour take presentyd kynge kynge wolde see hym sent hym london receyue iugement vpon saynt barthylme eue hangyd drawe hedesmyte bowelles take oute body brent body quarteres sent vnto foure best townes scotlonde heed put vpon spere sette vpon london brydge ensample scottes sholde haue mynde mysse ayenst ther lyege lorde eftsones phow scottes came kynge edwarde amende theyr done ayenst hym mygkelmas tho next comynge kynge edwarde helde parlemet westmester thy came scottes saye bysshop saynt andrewes robert brus erle caryk symonde frysell iohn erle athell accorded wt kynge boude othe swore afterwarde yf ony mysbare ayenst kynge edwarde sholde dysheryted euermore whan theyr pea thus made toke theyr leue pryuely went horne scotlonde phowe robert brus chalenged scotlonde roberte brus erle caryk sente hys letter erles baron scotlonde sholde come hym scone morowe concepcion lady grete edis lode lordes came day assygned day syr robert brus sayd fayre lordes full well ye knowe yts persone dwellyd ryght reame scotlonde ye wote well ryghtfull heyre syth syr iohn baylol oure kynge v hath forsake lefte londe though kynge edwarde englonde wt wronfull power hath made hym assent ayenst wyll yf yt ye wyl grau te may kynge scotlode shal kepe ayenst kynge edwarde enlonde ayenste manere men worde abbot scon arose vp sayde reason helpe hy ye londe kepe defende tho sayd presence al wolde geue hym thousand poude mayntene ye londe othere grauted londe hym wt ther power hym helpe defyed kynge edwarde englonde sayd robert brus sholde kynge englonde phow syr iohn comyn ayenst sayd crownynge syr robert brus lordynges sayd syr iohn comyn thynke truth othe ye made kynge edwarde englonde touchynge myselfe wyll nott breke myn othe man wente fro company ye tyme wherfore roberte brus tho hym consented wrothe menaced syr iohn
