pof syege tykhyll whan thomas erle lancastre herde wonder wrothe ther company greatly dyscomfyted ordeyned ther power togyder besyegyd yt castell tykhyll tho yt within manly defended yt baron myghte gete castell whan kynge herd yt castell besegyd swore god name yt sege shold remeued assembled huge power people went thederward rescowe castell power encresyd fro day day whan erle lancastre erle herforde baron ther copany herd thynge assebled theyr power went burto vpon trent kepte brydge yt kynge sholde passe ouer befell tenthe daye marche yere grace mcccxxi kyg spen er syr aymer valaunce erle penbroke iohn erle arun dell theyr power went ouer water dyscomfyted therle thomas company fled castel tetbury then went pountfret vyage deyed sire roger daumore thabbay tetbury tyme erle thomas traytour wt hym callyd robert holonde knyght yt erle brought vp nought nourysshed hym butrye yeue hy athousand marke londe yere somoche erle louyd hym myghte erles courte hym lyked bothe amonge hyghe lowe craftly theyf bare hym ayenst lorde yt trustyd vpon hym ony man lyue erle ordeyned letter go erledome lancastre make men aryse helpe hym vyage saye v hundred men arm y fals traytour came noo manere men warne ne make aryse helpe lorde whan fals traytour herde tell yt hys lorde dyscomfyted burton vppon trent fals traytour theyf stele away robbyd rauensdele lordes men came fro scofyture toke thezhors harneys slewe myght take came yeldyd hym kynge pwhan good erle thomas wyst bytrayed abasshed sayd hymself almyghty god myght robert holonde fyde hert betray syth louyd hym moche god well maye man se hym yt man may dysceyue nother rather tha yt trustyth moost vpo hath full euyll yeldyd mi goodnes worshyp haue hym done thrugh kyndnesse haue hym auauncyd made hym hyghe low makyth go hyghe vnto lowe yett shall deye euyll dethe pof scomfyture brurbrygge good erle thomas lancastre hufroy de bohoune erle herford baron yt theym toke cousell bytwene frere prechers poutfret tho thought thomas vpon traytour robert holonde sayd repreyf ala robert holond hathe betrayed aye red euyll shred comyn assent sholde go castell dunstanbrughe whiche perteyned therldo lancastre yt shold abyde ther tyl yt kynge foryeue male talent pbut whan good erle thomas herde answerd manere sayd lordes sayd yf go towarde north northen men woll saye yt go towarde ye scottes shall holden traytours cause dystauce bytwene kyng edwarde robert brus made kynge scotlonde therfore say touchynge myselfe wylle go ferder north owne castell poutfret pand whan syr roger clyfford herde arose vp anone wrathe drewe swerde hygh swore god almyghty holy name yf yt wolde go sholde hym slee noble gentyll erle thomas lacastre sore aferde sayd fayr syres wyll goo whether euere ye bydde tho went togyder north hadde viic army came burbrig whan syr andrew herkela north coutree thrugh ordynauce kynge kepe countree scotlonde herde tell howe thomas lancastre scofyted company burton vpon trent ordened hym stronge power sy symonde warde also tho shyref yorke met baron burbrugge anone brake brydge made tree pand whan syr thomas lancastre herde syr andrewe herkela broughte wt hym suche power sore adrad sent syr andrewe herkela hy spake sayd hym manere syr andrewe sayd ye may well vndersto de yt lorde yt kynge ladde mysgouerned moche fals cousell thrugh syr hugh spenser fad er syr hugh sone syr iohn erle arudell thrugh mayster roberte baldok fals pyllyd clerke yt kynges come dwellynge wherfore praye yt ye wylle come v power ye haue ordeyned helpe dystroye venym englond traytours ben therin wyll yeue vnto best parte fyue erldoms yt haue holde wyll make vnto othe wyll neuer thynge wt counsell ye shall eft well wt v euer robert holonde tho answerd syr andrew herkela sayd syr thomas yt wolde ne consent therto manere thynge wt wyll comaudemet lorde kynge shold holden tratour euer whan yt noble erle thomas lacastre saw wolde consent hy maner thyg syr andrew sayd wyll ye cosente dystroye venymme reame consente atte one worde syr andrewe tell yere begoon ye shall take holde traytour ony holde v nowe worse dethe ye shall deye e er dyd ony knyghte englonde vnderstonde welle ye dyde neuer thynge sorer ye shall repente go doo good lykyth wyll put mercy god went fals traytour tyraut fals forsworn man thrugh noble erle thomas lancastre receyued army chyualrye thrughe hym made knyghte tho myghte men see archer draw one syde knyghtes also fought tho togyder wonder sore also amonge al humfroy de boughon erle herforde worthy knyght renoune thrugh cristendome stode fought enmyes vppon brydge ye noble lorde stode fought vpon brydge theyf rybaude sculkyd vnder brydge fyersly spere smote noble knyght udement yt bowellys came aboute fete ther ala sorow pyte slayne floure solace comforth also curteysye pand syr roger clyfforde noble worthy knyghte stode euer fought well worthyly hym defended noble baron atte laste sore woundyd heed syr wyllyam sullayande syr roger benefelde slayne batayll whan syr andrewe herkela saw yt syr thomas men lancastre lassed slakyd anone company came vnto gentyll knyght syr thomas layd vnto hym hygh voyce yelde traytour yelde gentyll erle thomas lancastre answerd thenne sayd nay lordes traitours ben none wyll neuer v yelde whyle lyues last leuer hadde slayne truth yelde v vnto syre andrewe ayen gardyd vppon syr thomas company yellynge crienge lyke wode wulf yelde traytours taken yelde sayd hyghe voys beware syres none hardy vppon lyfe lymme tomysdo thomas body lancastre worde good erle thomas yede castell sayd knelynge vpon knee torned vysage towarde crosse sayd almyghty god yelde holy putte vnto thy mercy vylaines rybaudes lept abowte hym euery syde tyrautes wood torme tour dyspoyled hym armoure clothed hym robe ray yt squyres lyueray forthe ladde hym vnto yorke water tho myght men see moche sorowe care gentyll knyghtes fledde euery syde rybaudes vyllayns egerlye th dyscryed cryed hygh yeld traytours yelde whan yelden robbyd bouden theuys ala ye shame dyspyte gentyll ordre knyghthode batayll lode tho without lawe holy chirche tho nomore ereuerence burdell hous batayll fader ayenst sone ye vncle ayest neuewe somoche vnkyndnesse neuer seen englonde tyme amonge folkes one nacyon one kynred pyte hungry wulf hath shepe wonder greate lordes englonde one nacyon medlyd othere nacyons saye brytons saxon danys pehypes frensshemen norman spanyerdes romayns henaude soom flemynges othere dyuers nacyons whyche nacyons accordyd notte kynde bloodeof englonde yf greate lordes weddyd englysshe people thenne sholde pea haue ben reste amonge theym without ony enuye yt batayll roger clyfforde take syr iohn monbrey syr wyllyam tuc syr wyllyam fitz wyllyam many worthy knyghtes take batayll syr hugh dandell nexte daye taken put pryson sholde haue doon dethe yf spousyd ye kynges nece yt erle gylbertes systre gloucestre anone syr berthylmewe badelesmore take stow parke maneyr bysshop lyncoln yt neuewe many baron baronettes wherfor made noche sorowe phow thomas lancastre hee dyd pountfret v baron hangyd drawen shall telle noble erle thomas lancastre whan take brought yorke many cyte full gladde vpon hym cryed hygh voys syre traytoure ye welcome blessyd god ye shall haue rewarde longe ye haue deserued cast vpon hym many snowe balles many repreues dyd hym gentyll erle al suffred sayd nother word pand tyme ye kynge herde scomfyture ful glad ioyous grete haste came poutfret syr hughe spenser syr hughe sone syr iohn erle arundell syr edmonde wodestoke ky ge brother erle kent syr aymer valaunce erle penbroke mayster robert baldoke fals pyllyd clerke yt pryue dwelled kynges court came theder kynge kynge entryd castell syr andrew herkela fals tyraunte thrugh kynges comaundement toke hym gentyll erle thomas pountfret ther prysoned owne castell newe made stode ayenst abbaye kynge edwarde pand syr hugh spenser fad er sone caste thought howe manere good erle thomas lancastre sholde deed without iu gement perys wherfore ordeyned thrugh kynges iusticys kynge sholde put vpon hym poyntes treason befell ledde barre kynges iustices bareheed theyf fayre halle owne castell yt hadd made therin many fayre feste bothe ryche poore pand iustices syr hughe spenser fader aymer valaunce erle penbroke syr edmonde wodstok erle kent syr iohn brytayne erle rychemonde syr obert malemethrop iustyce syr robert hym acouspyd manere ptho ma court excludeth manere answer thomas lorde kynge puttyth vpon yt ye haue lond ryden baner dysplayed ayenst hys pea traytour pand word gentyll erle thomas hygh voyce sayd nay lordes forsoth aynt thomas neuer traytoure pthe iustice sayd ayen tho thomas lorde kynge puttythe vpon ye haue robbyd folke murdred people theyf thomas also kynge puttythe vpon dyscomfyted people folke owne reame wherfore ye went fledde woode annutlaw thomas traytoure ye shall hangyd reason kynge hath foryeuen iugemente loue quene isabell thomas reson wolde yt ye sholde hangyd kynge hath foryeue iugemet cause loue lygnage asmoche thomas ye taken fleenge outlawe kynge woll heed shall smyten anone haue hym pre brynge hym hys iugement pwhan thelgen tyll knyght thomas herde thyse wordes hygh voyce cryed sore wepynge sayd ala saynt thomas fayr fader ala shall deed th graunte nowe blessydfull god answere auayled hym thynge cursyd gascoyns put hym hyther thyther hym cryed wt hyghe voys kynge arthur moost terryble dredefull well knowen shewed nowe thyne open traytour euyll dethe shalt thou ryghte anone deye haste thou ryghte well deserued pand thenne thyse cruell folke sette vpon ye gode knyght thomas scorne olde chaplet rent yt worth halfe peny sette hym vpon white palfroy ful vnsemely also bara olde brydell horryble noyse draue hym castell towarde dethe caste vppon hym many balles snow dyspyte traytours lad hym castell tho sayd pyteous wordes hys hondes helde vp hygh towarde heue kynge heuen yeue v merci erthly kynge hath v forsaken frere precher went hym castell tyll came place ended lyfe vnto whome shroue hym lyfe gentyll erle helde frere wonder faste clothes sayd hym fayr fader abyde v tyll yt deed flesshe quakyth drede dethe pand sothe saye gentyll erle set hym vpon knee torned hym towarde eest rybaude yt called hygone mostoon sette honde vpon gentyll erle sayd dyspyte hym syr traytour torne towarde scottes thy fowle dethe receyue torned towarde north noble erle thomas answered tho mylde voys sayd nowe fayr lordes shall wyll worde frere went hym sore wepynge anone rybaude went hym smote heed xi kalendas auerell ye yere grace mcccxxi palas euer suche gentyll blood sholde deth withouten cause reason traytoursly ye kynge couseylled whan thrugh fals counseylle spenser suffred syr thomas vncles sone put suche dethe beheeded ayenst manere reason greate pyte also suche noble kynge sholde dysceyued mysgouerned thrugh counseyll fals spenser whiche tho mayntened thrughe loselry ayenst honour alsoo proffyte afterwarde ther fell grete vengaunce englonde bycause forsayd thomas deth pwhane gentyll erle lyfe passyd pryour monkys pounfret gate body syr thomas kyng buryed hyghe awter ryght syde pthat day thys gentyll knyght dede hangyd drawen quarell poutfret syr wyllyam tuchet syr wyllyam fitz wyllam syr werreyn isell syr henry bradborn syr wyllyam cheyne baron iohn page esquyer sone yorke drawen hangyd syr roger clyfforde syre iohn mambray baron syr goseline deuyll knyght pand brystowe drawen hangyd syr henry wemyngton syr henry mountforde baron pand gloucetre drawen hangyd syr iohn gaffarde syr wyllyam elmebrugge baron london gangyd drawen syr henry tyes baron pand wynchel se sye thomas clepepyr knyght ferthermore tell cruell occyon wyndsore drawe hangyd syr frauncys waldenham baron cau terbury drawen hangyd syre badeles syr barthyl ew asshe baron cardyf walys syr wyllyam flemmynge baron phow kynge edwarde went scotlonde hundred thousande men army myght spede whanne kynge edwarde englonde brought floure cheualry vnto theyr dethe thrughe sounsell consent syr hugh spenser fader syr hugh sone became woode ony lyon soo euer spenser wolde haue done well kynge louyd theym myght hym thynge yt lyked wherfore kynge gaaf vnto sir hugh spenser ye fader erldom wy chestre vnto syr andrewe herkela theerldom cardoill preiudyce harmynge crowne kynge edwarde tho thrugh cousell spe sers dysheryted yt ayenst hym ony quarell wt thomas la castre many dysheryted also bycause spenser coueyted haue theyr lode wolde desyre wro ge ayenste reason tho made kyg robert baldok false pylled clerke chaunceler englond thrugh cou sell forsayd spenser pand false rybaude coueytouse counseylled kynge moche kyng lete take owne warde goodes lordes put wronfully dethe owne honde aswell toke ye godes within holy chirche godes yt without lete theym put tresoury london lete calle forfeytes ther cou sell kynge wroughte euer dy heryted godes oughte thrugh ther counsell lete er legge goodes englonde wherfore rychest kynge euer englonde wyllyam bastarde yt cuonquered englonde yet thrughe cousell hym semyd notte ynough made yet euery toune englonde fynde man army vpon theyr owne costes go werre vpon scottes yt hys enmyes wherfore kynge wente scotlonde h udred thousande men army wytsontyde yere oure lorde ihesu criste mcccxxii scottes wente hyd mouteyns wodes taryed englysshmen fro day day kynge myght manere thynge fy de playne felde wherfore englysshmen lytyll vytaylles deyed hungre wonder faste sodenly goynge comynge namely tho ben ayenst thomas lancastre robbyd men vpon londes whan kynge edwarde saw vytaylles fayled hym wonder sore dyscomfited bycause also yt men deyed myght pede enmyes laste came ayen englonde anone came iames douglas also thomas rudulph huge hooste englonde northumberlonde englysshmen dryuen oute englonde came robbyd cou tree slewe people also bree towne yt callyd northallerton many townes yorke wha kynge herde tydynges lete mone manere men myght traueyller englysshmen mette scottes abbay beyg elande xv daye myghelmas yere aboue sayd englysshe men dyscomfyted atte scomfyture take syr iohan brytayne erle rychmonde helde countre erldom lancastre payed huge raunsome lete god wente fraunce came neuer agayne phow syr andrew herkelay take put deth yt erle cardoil tyme syr andrew herkela yt new made erle cardoil cause yt taken good erle thomas lancastre phe ordeyned thrugh kynges comau dement englonde brynge hy power myght helpe ayenst scottes abbaye beyghlande whan fals traytour gadred people myght sholde haue come kynge vnto abbaye beyghelande fals traytour ladde nother coutre thrughe copelonde thrughe therldome lancastre wente thrugh countre robbyd slew folke yt myghte ferthermore fals traytour take grete e golde sylue syr iamys douglas ayenste kynge englonde helpynge holdynge scottes thrugh whose treason kynge englonde scomfyted beyghlande came f yder wherfore kynge toward hym wonder wrothe lete pryuely enquere coutre abowte yt men enquered aspyed laste trough foude soughte atteynte take fals traytour gode erle thomas lancastre hym tolde yt put vnto deth takynge burbrugge sayd yere doon sholde take holde traytour holy man sayd pwherfore ky ge sente pryuely syr anthoyn lucy knyghte countre cardoil yt shold take syr andrewe herkela put hym vnto dethe bryge thynge vnto ende kynge sente commyssyon yt andrewe take cordoil ladde vnto barre manere erle worthyly arayed swerde gyrde hym hosyd sporyd ptho spake syr authoyn maner syr andrew sayd kynge puttyth vpon asmoche thou hast orpyd thy de dy dyd moche honoure made erle cardoil thou traytour thy lorde laddest peple countre sholde haue holpe hym att bataylle beyghelande thou laddest away countre copelonde thrugh erldom lancastre wherfor lorde kynge discomfy scottes thrugh thy treason falsnesse yf haddest come bi tymes batayll treason thou didest gre gold syluer thou receyued iamys douglas scot kyng enmye lorde kynge wyll ordre knyghthode whiche receyued thyne honoure shyp vpon thy body brought nought thyn estate vndoyne knyghtes lower degree mowe ware whiche lorde hath auaunted hugely dyuerse countres englonde maye take ensample ther lorde afterwarde truly serue ptho commaunded anone knaue hew spore helys lete breke swerde ouer heed whiche kynge yaue hym kepe defende londe therwith whanne made hym erle cardoyll lete hym vnclothed furred taberd hode furryd cote gyrdyll wha ne done syr anthony sayd ne vnto hym andrewe sayd nowe art thou knyght knaue thy treason kynge wyll thou shal hangyd drawen thy heed thy bowel take thy body brent thy body quartryd thy heed sente londo shal stonde vpon london brydge foure quarter shall sent foure townes englonde yt may beware chastised anthony sayd done manere thynge ye laste daye octobre yere grace miijcxxii yere sonne torned blood people sawe dured morne tyll xi clocke pof miracle yt god wroughte saynt thomas lancastre wherfore kynge lete closein ye chirche dores pryory pountfret yt man shold come therin offre sone good erle thomas lancastre martryd preest longe tyme blynde dremed slepe yt sholde go hyll good erle thomas lancastre doon vnto dethe sholde haue syght ayen dremed thre nyghtes sewynge preest lete lede hym hyll whan came place martryd full deuowtly made prayer prayed god saynt thomas myght haue syghte ayen prayer layed ryght honde vpon place gode man martryd drope drye blood smale sonde cleuyd honde therwith stryked eyen anone thrughe myght god saynt thomas lancastre hadde syghte ayen thankyd tho almyghtye god saynt thomas whanne miracle knowen amonge men people came thyther euery syde knelyd made theyr prayer atte hys tombe pryory poutfret prayed holy martyr socour helpe god herde ther prayer palso yonge chylde drowned well towne pountfret deed thre dayes thre nyghtes men came layed deed chylde vpon sayd thomas tombe holy martyr chylde arose dethe lyfe many man sawe pand also moche people oute ther mynde god sent theyr mynde ayen thorough vertue holy man pand god hath yeue also cry pyls theyr goynge crokyd thyr hondes ther fete blynde also syght manyseke folke ther helth dyuers maladyes loue gode martyr palso ryche man cou dom gascoyne suche malady ryghte syde rotyd fell awaye hym men myghte see lyuer herte stanke vnneth myght come n gh hym wherfore frendes wonder sory last god wolde prayed saynt thomas castre wold pray almyghty god prysoner yght go pountfret theyr pylgrymage thoughte martyr saynt thomas came hym anoynted hys syke body therwith gode man awoke hoole flesshe restored ayen rotyd fallen away whiche myracle good man frendes louyd god saynt thomas euermore good man came englonde toke hym foure felowe came poutfret holy martyr dyd theyr pylgrymage gode man syke came thyther nakyd sauf preuye clothes whan done torned home ayen theyr owne countre tolde miracle wheresoeuer came pand also two men haue heelyd mormale thrugh helpe holy martyr though yt euyll holde curable whan spenser herde god dyd suche miracle holy man nolde byleue manere wyse sayd openly yt gret resye suche vertue hym byleue whan syr hugh spenser sone sawe al doynge anone sent messager poutfret yt dwelled ky edwarde yt tho grauen scypton cause yt kynge sholde vndo pylgrymage rybaude messager went towarde kynge message came hylle good martyr doon dethe place made ordure whan done rode towarde ye kynge stronge flyxe came vpon hym came yorke tho shed hys bowelles fudment whan sir hugh spenser herde tydynges dele adradde thoughte vndo pylgrymage yf myghte ony manere waye anone went kynge sayd yt shold grete sklaudre thrugh crystendome deth thomas lancastre yt suffred people ther pylgrymage poutfret couseled kynge yt comauded shyt chirche dores poutfret chirche holy martyr enterid thus dyd ayenste frauchyses holy chirche foure yere myght pylgryme come holy bodye bycause monkes suffred men come honoure yt holy bodye saynt thomas ye martyr thrugh cou sell syr hugh spenser sone thrughe cousell mayster robert baldok fals pylled clerke yt kyng chau celer yt kynge consented yt shold sette theyr wage lete make warde yn ouer ther owne good longe tyme thorough commaundement forsayd syr hughe spenser xiiii gascoynes well armyd kept hylle ther good man saynt thomas vnto deth pylgrym myght come way full well went haue take cristis myght hys power grete boo miracle shewed martyr saynt thomas thrugh al crystendom tyme kyge made robert baldok false pylled clerke thrughe prayere syre hugh spenser sone made chauseler englonde tyme castell walyngforde holden ayenste kynge thrugh prysoners within castell saynt thomas loue lancastre wherfore people coutre came toke castell prysoners wherfore syr iohan goldyngton knyght syr edmonde becche prysoners taken sent vnto kynge pountfret done pryson yt sayd roger sent vnto yorke drawen hangyd anone syr roger mortymer wygmo brake oute toure london manere forsayd roger de sholde drawe hangyd atte lo morow saynt laurece dai daye helde fayre feste toure london syr stephen segraue conestable tour many grete men wt whan ther sholde soupe forsayd stephen sete officer tour came souped wt hym whan sholde take ther leue hy squyre yt callyd stephe yt full preuy forsaid rogere thrugh cousell yaue al suche drynke yt leest slepe two dayes two nyghtes meane tyme escaped awaye water tamys went ouer see helde hym fraunce wherfore kynge sore anoyed put stephen constabelery phow quene isabell wente fraunce treate pea bytwene lorde kynge englonde kynge fraunce broder kynge wente tho vnto londo thrugh counsell syr hugh spenser fader sone mayster robert baldok fals pylled clerke chaunceler lete sease thoo londes hondes also londes yt syr edwardes sone put theyr wagys ayenst maner reson yt thrughe falsnesse spenser pand whan kynge fraunce yt quene isabelles brother herde falsnesse sore anoyed ayenst kynge englonde fals counsellers wherfore sent letter kynge edwarde vnder seale yt sholde come certaine daye homage therto oned hym el shold lese gascoyne ordeyned englo de thrugh kynge cousell quene isabell sholde goo fraunce treate pea bytwene lorde broder olyuer yngham sholde go gascoyne haue hym vij men army moo seneschall wardeyne gascoyne ordeyned yt quene isabell came frauce wente syr aymer valaunce erle penbroke murdred sodenly preuysege yt thrugh goddes vengauce one iusticys yconsented saynt thomas deth lancastre wolde neuer repent hym wyckyd dede tyme syr olyuer yngham went ouer gascoyne dyd moche harme kyng frauce gate ayen kynge edwarde lost moche therto phow kyng edwarde sent syr edwarde sone eldest fraunce quene isabell quarter yere dwelled fraunce whan syr edwarde eldest sone axyd leue tho go frauce speke moder isabell quene fader kynge grautyd hym good wyll sayd hym go fayre sone goddys blessynge myn thynke come ayen hastely maye wente ouer see frauce kynge frauce vncle receyued hym moche honoure sayd vnto hym fayr sone ye welcome cause yt fader come homage duchye guyon au cetourrs wont yeue yt lordshyp holde tage maner aucetours dyde wherfore callyd duke guyon phowe kynge exyled quene ysabell edwarde eldest sone kynge edwarde englonde herd tell kyng frau ce yeue chye guyon vnto sir edwarde sone without consent wyll hym yt sone receyued duchye became wonder wrothe sent sone pwhan quene herde thyse tydynges sore adradde dystroyed thrugh fals coniectynge spenser went knyghtes exyled englonde saynt thomas cause lancastre saye syr roger wig syr wellyam trussell syr hohn wolde auenged euer toke pit longe afterwarde kynge edwarde dame phylyp wyf dame isabell kynges moder syre rogere mortimer ne went vnto notyngham sotourne befell quene isabell thrughe couseyll mortymer fre de muste herberowed castell mortimer went toke theyre herberowe dyuerfe place towne notyngham tho sore aferde leest mortimer sholde theym dystroye hast came vnto kyng edwarde syr wyllyam moutagu thousande artbers fote men tho went shyppe atte raue spore sayled see tyl came vnto scotlond came lo de kynkehorne xii myle fro saynt iobannes towne anone sent shyppes agayne sholde hurte ne empeyred neyther noo man sholde go shyppes agayn though nede abyde alperylles flee stonde rather suffre dethe flee mayntene theyr true quarell whan erle fysse fyers man sterne herde bayllol come take londe full ruyl ashamyd lytyll company bad hym dyscomfyted shamefully putt hym company alyue flee ptho came syr edwarde bailloll toke countree aboute hym tyll came vnto abbay du fermlin founde vitaylles hym people nowe dere lordes ye knowe full well ben lodged bytwene enmyes may v hampre bote deth wherfore yf abyde styll nyght wene shal torne v moche harme power scotlonde may euery wexe encre e may ben atte hangynge bough moore straite passage faste hastyd vnto englysshmen thousand felle onto grounde echone ouer vpon hepe bothe hors man bayllol men myghtylye stode ayenste theym faste slewe scottes englysshe mystrels blewe theyr tru pet theyr claryons hydously ascryed scottes tho euery englysshe batayll two wynges price archer batayll shot arowes fast sore scottes myght helpe themself scottes thousandes vnto grou de began flee fro englysshmen saue theyr lyues whane scottes knaues saw scomfyture scottes fall faste grou de pryckyd fast theyr maysters horse sporys kepe theym peryll sette theyr maysters force whan thenglysshmen sawe lept theyr horse faste pursued scottes abode slewe downe ryghte pthere men myghte see doughtynesse noble kynge edwarde men manly pursewed scottes flow mcccxxxii pand doynge lastyd englyssh page toke pylfre scottes slayne euery man myght take without ony chalengynge ony man gracyous vyctory kyng tornyd hym agayne vnto syege berewyk pand whanne syeged hym god passed ayen oute englonde pand yere kynge rycharde ryall power te scotlonde warre vpon scottes falsnes destruccyon scottes done vnto englysshmen march thanne scottes come downe kynge treate rycharde othere squyre called iohn walssh poy te treason nauerne put vpon walssheman nauerne ouercomen yelde hym recreaunt aduersary anone dyspoyled armure drawen ont palays tyburne hanged falsnes pand xiiii yere kynge rychardes regne syr iohn gaut duke lancastre wente ouer see spayne chalenge ryght wyfes tytle vnto crowne spayne greate host peple men armes archer hym duchesse wyfe thre doughters ouer see spayne greate whyle laste kynge spayne began treate duke lancastre accorded togyder thrugh theyr couseyll manere kynge spayne sholde wedde duke doughter lancastre ryght heyre spayne hym touchynge tytle ryght normandye gascoyne guyhen whiche kynge frau ce withelde wrongfully vnryghtfully whiche aucestres hym trewe tytle conquest ryght herytage whiche normandye gascoyn guyhen good kynge edwarde wyndesore aucestres hy holden theyr lyues tyme lordes gaaf hym couseyll sende enbassatours vnto kynge fraunce hys counseyll sholde gyue vp vnto hy ryght herytage yt saye norma dye warre ayenste hym lyke yet good warryour make suche conqueste vpon hym somwhat scorne despyte sente hym toune full tenes balles bycause wolde haue somwhat playe hym lordes yt wolde become hym better mayntene ony warre pand anone oure lordes enbassatours toke theyr leue came englonde ayen tolde kinge counseyll vngoodly answere dolphyn present whiche sent oure kynge pand whan kynge herde theyr wordes answere dolphyn wonder sore agreued ryght euyll apayed towarde frensshmen towarde kynge dolphyn thought auenge hym sone god wolde sende hym gace myght anone lete make tenes alles dolphyn hast myght greate gon stone dolphyn playe anone kynge sent lordes helde greate counseyll westmynster tolde vnto swere dosphyn worthy present yt sent hym lordes playe ther kynge lordes accorded shold redy armes wt ther power best araye yt myght done gete men armes archer yt myght goten stuff longed warre redy wt theyr retenue mete southampon lammasse next folowyng without ony delay wherfore kynge ordeyned nauye shyppes maner stuffe vytayll longed suche wartyoure maner ordeynaunce hauen southampton nombre cc c xx saylles felle ther greate dysease foule mychef thre lordes whiche kyng trusted moche thrugh fals couetyse purposed ymagyned ky ge dethe thought haue slayne bretherne taken see whiche thre lordes named th slir rychard erle cambrydg b det duke yorke ye seconde lorde scrop tresourer englonde thyrde syr thomas gray knyghte north countree thre lordes afore sayd lucre money hadde made promesse vnto frensshe men haue slayne kynge henry fyft brethern fals trayne sodaynly hadde ware god almyghty helde holy honde ouer saued frome peryllous menye haue done receyued frensshmen myllyon golde yt openly knowen theyr fals treason thre iuged vnto dethe iugement sholde ladde thrugh hampton withoute north gate heded thus ended theyr lyues theyr false couetyse treason anone done kynge menye made redy went shyppes saylled forthe xv hondred shxppes aryued wt seyn kydecause vpon ladyes euen assumpcyon normandye wt ordynaunce soo wente hym forth harflet besyeged towne abowte londe elre water sent capytayne towne charged hym delyuer towne capytayne sayd wolde delyuer hym none ne none wold hym yelde badde hym best kynge layd ordynaunce vnto towne saye gonne engynnes trypgettes shotten caste walles eke vnto towne caste downe bothe towres towne layd theym vnto erthe played tentes harde gonstones pand within towne whan sholde playe theyr songe well awaye ala yt euer suche tenes balles made cursyd tho warre began tyme yt euer borne pand morne kynge dyd crye euery gate towne euery man sholde redy morneerly make assaute vnto towne wyllyam boucher iohn graunte xii burgeys worthy men came kynge sought hym ryall pryncehode power draw malyce destruccyon yt dyd besought hym viii dayes respyte trewes yf ony rescowe myght come theym el yelde vp towne vnto hy theyr goodes kyng senf forth capytayne kept remenaut styll wt hym lorde gauco e yt capytayne towne went forth royn ye haste vnto dolphy helpe socour none n man rescowe dolphyn wolde abyde thus cap tayne come ayen vnto kynge yelded vp towne delyuered hrm keyes hadde hym go putte frensshmen men woman chyldren stuff towne harflet englysshe people kynge sent englonde dyd crye euery go de towne englonde man wolde come thyder hym towne sholde haue house housholde hym hys heyres euer th de many dyuerse marchauntes men enhabyte theym towne welcome pand whan kynge sawe towne well stuffed bothe vytayls men worthy prynce toke leue went lalays warde londe frenssh men herde comynge thought haue stopped hym sholde passe waye hast myghte b al en brydges ony passage hors man soo moche remyghte noo man passe ouere ryuers nothere horse ne foote yf sholde haue drenchyd therfore oure kynge wt people wente sough way fer vp parys warde ryall power frau ce assembled redy gyue hym batayll dystroye people almyghty god guyde saued hym menye defended hym enmyes power purpose thanked god saued soo owne knyghte kynge ryghtfull tytle p kynge beholdynge seynge grete multytude nombre enmyes withstande waye gyue hym batayll kynge meke herte good spyryte lyfte vp hondes almyghty god besoughte hym helpe socoure daye saue trewe seruauntes kynge gadred lordes people aboute bad gode chere sholde haue fayre daye gracyous vyctorye better theyr enemyes prayed make redy vnto batayll wolde rather deed yt daye felde take enmyes wolde neuer put reame englonde rausome persone pand duke yorke fell knes besought kynge bone wolde graunte hym daye auautwarde batayll kynge grauted hym askynge sayd gramercy cosyn yorke prayed hym make hym redy bad euery man ordeyne hym stake tree sharpe endes stake myght pyght ye erthe slope theyr enemyes sholde ouercome theym horsbacke yt ther fals purpose arayed ouer ryde menye sodaynly fyrst comynge fyrst brunte nyght batayll frensshe men made many greate fyers moche reuell howtyng showtynge playd kynge lordes dyse archer alwaye blanke theyre moneye wende ben theyrs morne arose daye ganne sprynge kynge goode auyse lete araye batayll wynges charged euery man kepe hole gyder prayed goode chere whan redy asked tyme day sayd pryme sayd kynge nowe good tyme englonde prayed v therfore good chere lete v go iourney thanne sayd hygh voys name almyghty god saynt george auaute baner saynt george daye thyn helpe pand frensshemen came pryckynge downe wolde haue ouer ryden onre menye god archer made ryght sone stomble archer shote neuer arowe amysse perysshed brought vnto grounde bothe hors man shote daye wager stake made theym toppe ouer terue eche one ouer laye hepes twoo speres lenthe hyghte oure kynge menye men armes archer sthacked soo thycke arowes layd staues oure kynge hondes foughte manly daye thus god almyghty saynt george brought enmyes groude gaf v day vyctory slayne frensshmen daye felde agyngcourt mo xi thousande wt prysoners taken nombred daye frensshmen ye felde mo syx score thousade god day faught v came tydynges oure kynge newe bataylle frensshmen ordeyned redy stele hym came towardes hym pand anone oure kynge lette crye euery man sholde doo sle prysoners hadde taken anone make theym ayen redy fyghte wyth frensshe men whan thei sawe oure men kylled downe theyr prysoneres thanne dyde wythdrawe brake theyr batayll araye thus kynge worthy conquerour daye vyctory felde agyngcourte pycardye kynge reforned ayen ther batayll see people slayne englysshmen ony hurte myghte holpen dede felde duke barrye duke alausome duke braban yerle nauerne chy ef censtable frauce viii erles ye archebysshop sauce gode baros hondred moo worthy knytes greate alyauce cote armures thousande v hondred englysshmen deed daye good duke yorke erle southfolke englysshmen deed passyge xxvi bodyes tha ked god batayll frydaye whiche saynt cryspyne cryspynyanes daye monethe octobre anone kynge commau ded bury duke yorke caryed forth hym erle southfolke prysoneres duke orlyauce duke burbon erle vendome erle ewe erle rychemonde syre bursygaut marchall frauce many worthy lordes taken thys batayll agyngcourt brought vnto towne calays ouer see ye kynge englonde landed douer kent prysoners saufte thanked god almyghty came caunterbury offred saynt thomas shryne rode forth thrugh countre kent next waye vnto eltham restted tyll wolde come london mayer london alderman shreues worthy comuners craftes came blacke hethe well worthely arayed welcome kynge dyuerse melodyes thanked almyghty god hys gracyous vyctory shewed hym kynge prysoners passed forth theym tyll came saynt thomas waterynge met hym relygyous men processyon welcomed hym kynge came rydinge wt prysoners thrugh cyte lo shewed many fayre fyght conduytes crosse chepe heuenly araye angelles ar chaugelles patrya kes prophetes virgynes wt dyuerse melodyes sensynge syngynge welcome kyng ye conduytes rennynge wt wyne kynge passed forth saynt poules met wt hym xiiii bysshops euessed mytred sensers welcome kyng songe gracyous vyctory te deum laudamus kynge offred toke hors rode westmynster mayer toke leue kynge rode home ayen pand thyrde yere kynge henryes regne fyfth come emperoure almayne kynge rome hungrye englonde cyte london mayer alderman shreues worthy craftes london kynges comaudement met hym blacke heth best araye coude welcomed hym brought hym vnto london moche honoure greate reuerence saynt thomas waterynge met wt hym kynge lordes gode araye worthy metynge bytwene emperoure kynge ry fyfth kyssed togyder enb aced eche kyng toke emperoure honde soo came rydyng thrugh cyte lo vnto saynt poules ther alyghted offred alle bysshoppes stode reuesshed sensers theyr ondes sensynge theym toke theyr horse rode vnto westmy ster kynge lodged emperour owne palays rested hym greate whiche kyng coste pand soone came duke hollonde englonde come se emperoure speke hym kynge henry englonde worthyly receyued lodged bysshops inne ely kynges coste pand whan emperour hadde well rested hym seen londe dyuerse partyes knewe commodytees processe tyme toke leue kynge yode made knyght garter receyued wered lyueray thanked kynge lordes kynge wente ouer see vnto calays aboden longe tyme haue answere frensshe kynge laste came pleased hym ryghte noughte emperoure toke leue kinge passed forth goodes name kynge came ouer ayen englo de hast myghte saynt lucas euen came lambythe mondaye nexte came parleament westmynster pand yere grete derth corn englonde thanked god lasted longe fourth yere kynge henryes regne fyfth held parlemente westmynster begynynge octobre last puryfycacyon lady nexe grauted vnto hym mayntene warres spyrytualtee teporalte hole taxe dyeme thrugh cyte takynge leue maner people well pore ryche praynge theym generall praye hym rode forth saynt george fred toke leue mayer charginge hym kepe well chambre rode forth hampton ther abode tyll thanne kynge herynge many enemyes vppon see saye ix greate carackes hulkes galays shyppes comynge dystroye nauye anone commaunded erle marche chyef chyeftayne many worthy lordes hym men armes archer go se none enmyes defouled nauyene entred londe partye dystroble vyagene iourney anone erle toke menye went shyp scommed see kept see costes manere enmyes durste rowte vpon see anone kynge sente knyght bathe ther syr lowys robert salyn chaynye mougomerye many worthy men kynge commauded put frensshmen woman man hardy defoule woman ne take maner good awaye frame theym lette passe pea payne xxi daye monthe quene came xxiiii crowned westmynster palso yere anone ester kynge helde parlement westmy ster atte whiche parlement ordeyned golde englysshe coyn sholde weyed none receyued weyghte anone wytsontyde kynge saylled calays passed forth fraunce xxii daye marche kynge came ouer duke clarence slayn frauce dyuerse lordes taken prysoners erle huntyngdon erle somerset dyuerse al bycause wolde nott take none archer theym thought haue ouercome frensshmen themselfe wt archer yet whan slayne archer came rescowed body duke whiche wolde haue caryed god haue mercye soule valyaunt man yere bytwene crystmasse delmasse towne mylon yolden vnto kynge pin ix yere saynt nycholas daye decembre borne henry kynges fyrste begoten sone wyndesore who godfaders attthe font stone syr henry bysshop wynchestre iohn duke bedford duchesse holonde godmoder henry chychelay archebysshop cauterbury godfader confermynge pand x yere cyte mew bry goten whiche hadde ben longe beseyged yere quene shypped hampton sayled ouer kynge fraunce worshypfully receyued kynge also kynge frauce hir fader hir moder thus kynge henry wanne fast frauce helde grete astate sate greate feest parys crowned quene also whiche hadde seen people resorted vnto court kyng fraunce helde none astatene rule lefte almoost alone palso yere wedercoke set vppon poules steple london yere moneth august kynge waxed seke boy de vyncet whan saw sholde deye made testamet ordeyned many noble thynges soule deuoutelye receyued ryghtes holy chirche ferre forth whan anoynted sayd seruyfe wt preest verse psalme miserere mei deus benigne facdne bona voluntate tua syon vt edif centur mury iherusalem adde tarye sayd thus good lorde thou knowed myn entent hath ben yet yf myghte lyue reedyfye walles iherusalem thanne preest proceded forth made ende anone moost noble prynce vyctoryous kynge floure tyme crysten chyualrye whome worlde doubted gaf soule handes god deyed made ende naturall lyfe forsayd boy de vyncent besyde parys xxxvi yere aege vphon who soule god haue mery amen pthan body enbamed ceryd layd ryall chare ymage lyke hym layd vpon corp open wt dyuerse baners horse couered rychely armes englonde fraunce also olde armes saynt edwarde saynt edmonde grete multytude torch whome went ye kyng scotlonde many lordes whyche accompanyed body tyll came vnto westmynster london englond euery towne waye solepnely dyryge euen masse morne moche almes gyuen poore people waye vii day nouembre corp broughte thrugh london wt grete reuerence solempnyte westmyster lyeth worshypfully buryed layd tombe ryall ymage lyke hymself syluer gylde made coste quene katheryne thus ended entered buryed noble kynge henry fyfth vpon who soule crysten soules god haue mercy amen pof lawe kynge henry fyfth ordeyned kyng rycharde hymselfe dethe heere noted kynge henry fyfth noble ty ce kynge crowned yongth ben wylde recheles spared thynge luste ne desyres accoplysshed lykynge sone crowned enoynted sacred anone soda ly chaunged newe man set entent lyue vertuously maynte nynge holy chirche destroynge heretykes kepynge iustyce defend nge reame subgectes pand moche fader deposed abour good kynge rycharde pre ously made hym deye done hym ayenst legeauce sente rome assoyled therof whiche offence oure holy fader e pope enioyned hym make hym prayed perpetually lyke done taken frome hym naturall lyfe therfore sholde foude four taper b ene perpetually body ertynccon bodely lyf soule may euer remebred lyf heue spyrytuall lyfe also sholde euery weke daye come aboute dethe haue solempne masse requyem euen afore dy yge ix lesson doole poore people alwaye daye xi shellynges vii pen deled peny mele one yere annyuersarye termente holden moost honeste wyse deled daye xx pounde pen poore people euery monke xx shellynge whiche thynges performed noble kynge fader kynge henry fourth fader performed notte durynge lyfe wome sayd god dyd touche hym lep e deyed pand alsoo noble prynce lete doo calle abbottes pryours saynt b net order englonde chapytre hous west mynstre reformacyon theyr order wherin comunycacyon alsoo bysshops men spyrytualtee ferre forth doubted sore wolde haue hadde pemporaltees theyr hondes wherfore aduyse labour procurynge spyrytualte encouraged king chalenge normandye ryght frauce entent set hym awerke sholde seke none occasyons entre suche mater lyfe tyme afterwarde laboured besy warre nobly endowed dayly grete almes dedes chartre hous certayn chyldren founden scole syon certayn almes gyue dayly yet besyde fou ded recluse whiche shall alway preest praye hym sayd chartre hous whiche preest suffycyently endowed hym seruaunt lo maye prynces take ensample noble prynce regned lytyll tyme fully x yere dyd many noble actes well soule perpetually remembred prayed conquestes beynge moste wente pin yere reynolde pecok bysshop chestre foude heretyke thyrde daye decembre adiured lambeth presence archebysshop caunterbury many bysshoppes doctours lordes temporall bokes brent poules crosse pand ye haue herde howe certayne lordes slayne atte saynt albons wherfore alwaye grutchynge wrathe hadde heyres slayne ayenste duke yorke erles werwyk salysbury wherfore kynge aduys hys counseyll sente theym vnto london whiche place duke yorke came xxvi daye ianueri wt four hundred men lodged hym baynerdes castell owne place pand xv daye ianuer came erle salysbury v hundred men lodged therber owne place pand came duke excetre somerset wt viiic men laye withoute temple barre pand erle northu berlonde lorde egremonde lorde clyfforde xv hundred men lodged without towne pand mayre tyme geffraye boloyne kepte greate watche comyns cyte rode abowte cytce holborne fletestrete v thou sande men well arayed armyd kepe pea pand xiii day feuerer erle warwyk came london fro calays well beseen worshypfully v hundred men redde iakectes broudred ragged staff behynde lodged gray freres pand xv daye marche kynge came london quene accorde pea made among lordes set pea lady daye xv day marche yere lorde mcccclviii ye kynge quene lordes went processyon poules london anone kynge lordes departed yere grete fraye flete strete bytwene men courte men strete whiche fraye quenes attourney slayne phow kynges housholde made fraye ayenst erle werwyk iourneye bloreheth also yere erle werwyk couseyll west mynster kynges housholde meny gadred togyder haue slayne sayd erle helpe god frendes recouerde barge escapyd theyr euyll enterpryse well coke came rennynge spyttes pestels ayenst hym daye rode towardes warwyk sone gate hym commyssyon went ouer see towarde calays psone therle salysbury comynge london encoutred att bloreheth lorde audley people ordeyned dystroy hauynge knowlege sholde mette accompanyed two sone syr thomas iohan neuell grete felyshyp men faught togeter theerle salysbury lorde audley many gentylmen people hurte erles two hurte goynge homewarde taken quenes menye pafter calixt pius pope chose yere mcccc callyd eneas man poete embassatour emperour wrote noble treatyse also canoursed senys pope ordeyned dulgence pard de go werre ayenst te pystle greate turke hym become crysten ordeyned passage ayenstre ankon whiche mo ke people drewe partyes whiche people sence many home cause suff anone dyed sayd ankon yere oure lorde mcccclxiii xiiii daye august phow andrewe trollop soul dyours calays forsoke duke yorke theyr mayster therle warwyk weste countre duke yorke erles warwyk salysbury sawe ye gouernaunce reame stode mooste quene hir counseyll greate prynces londe callyd couseyll sett parte oonly sayd thrugh reame tho sayd lordes shold dystroyed openly shewed blorehethe wolde haue slayne erle salysbury sauacon theyr lyues also comyn wele reame thought remedy thyse thyng assembled togyder moche peple toke felde west countre whiche therle warwyk came fro calars wt many olde souldyours andrewe trollop whose wysdome werre trustyd moche vpon whan thus assembled made theyr felde kyng sent comyssyons preuy seales vnto lordes reame come wayte hym theyr moost beste defensable araye euery man came suche wyse kynge stronger people duke yorke therles werwyk salisbury notyd ye euery lorde englonde tyme durst dysobeye quene rulyd peasybly done abowt kynge whiche good well dyspoysed man whan kynge come place duke yorke felyshyp made theyr feld strongest wyse purposyd veryly abyde haue fouzte nyght andrwe trollop olde souldyours calays greate felyshyppe sodeynly departyd duke hoost wente strayte vnto kynges felde receyued ioyously knewe thentent thother lord also maner theyr felde duke yorke lordes seynge thez dysceyued toke counseyll shortly ye nyght departed frome felde leuynge behynde moste partye theyr people kepe felde tylle morowe duke york seconde sone departyd thrughe walys towarde irlonde leuynge eldest sone therle marche erles werwyk salysbury whiche rode togyder wt thre four persones strayght deuenshyre helpe ayde one denham gate shyp whyche coste xi score noble shyp sayled fro then gernescy refresshed theym frome then sayled calays recey ued castell postern towne wyst duke yorke toke shyppynge walys sayled ouere irlonde well receyued phow erles marche werwik salysbury entred calays erle werwyke wente irlonde kynge henry host felde notte knowynge sodeyne departynge morow foude none ye felde sayd lordes sent ye hast men folowe pursue take met god wolde kynge went ludlowe dyspoyled castell towne sent duchesse yorke chyldren duchesse bokyngham syster kept longe tyme forth kynge ordeyed duke somerset capytayne calays thyse lordes departed afore sayd proclamyd rebel greate traytours duke somerset toke hym souldyours departyd fro felde made hym redy hast go calays take possessyon offyce whanne came fonde therle werwyk therin capytayne erles marche salysbury also londed scalys went gynes receyued fortuned thoo shyppes came ouer hym came calays hauen ther fre wyll shypmen ought fauour therle werwyk duke somerset whiche shyppes take dyuerse men ienyn fynkyl iohan felowe kaylles purser whiche beheded sone calays came men dayly ouer thyse lordes calays began wexe stronger stronger borowed moche goode staple syde ye duke somerset beynge gynes gate people hym whiche came scarmysshed wyth theym calays calays whiche endured many dayes durynge skermysshynge moche peple came ouer dayly vnto thyse lordes pthen tyme thaduys counseyll lordes calays sente ouer mayster denham grete felyshyp sandwytche whiche toke towne therin ye lorde ryuers lorde scalys sone toke many shyppes hauen brought calays wt whiche shyppes many maryners ther fre wyll came calays serue therle werwyk erle werwyk aduys lordes toke shyppes manned theym wel sayled hymself irlonde speke duke yorke ke hys aduys sholde entre englond whan done erandes retorned aye towardes calays broughte hym moder countesse salysbury comynge weste countre seey duke excetre admirall englonde beynge grace du c copanyed wt many shypp werre met erle werwyk flete faught substauce peple beynge wt duke excetre ought better wyll fauoure erle werwyk hym departed came calays sauftee pthen kynges couseyll seynge thyse lord goten shyppes fro sandwhtche taken lorde ryuers ue ordeyned garyson sandwytche abyde kepe towne made one forde capytayne towne ye vytaylle ne marchaust shold ge unders sholde go calays thithes calays seynge made ham many go sandwytche sayled towne londe water brought capytayne ouer se smote heed yet dayly men came ouer theym fro partyes phow therle marche w wyk salysbur catred e tglonde felde northapton w ere dyuerse lordes llayne forsayd erles marche warwyk salysbur came ouer douer moche people londed whome count e drewe came london armyd lete lordes kynges cousell knowe theyr truth also entente assembled theym tolde theym entended harme kyng persone sauf wolde put frome hym suche persones hym departed frome london wyth grete puyssaunce towarde northampton kynge accompanyed wt many lordes made stronge felde withoute towne partyes met fought greate batayll whyche batayll llayne duke bokyngham therle shrewesbury vycount beamonde lorde egremonde many knyghtes squyres also ky ge hymself taken felde afterwarde brought london none parlement westmy ster durynge whiche parlement duke yorke came irlonde ye erle rutlonde rydynge greate felyshyp palays atte westmynster toke kynges palays came parlement chambre toke kynges place claymyd ye crowne propre enherytauuce ryghte caste forth wrytynge tytle also ryghtfull heyre wherfor moche doo conclusyon appoynted cocluded ye kyng henry sholde regne kynge durynge naturall lyfe moche hadde kynge longe possessyd dethe duke yorke shold kynge heyres kynges hym forth wt sholde proclamyd heyre apparaut shold also protectour regete englonde durynge kyng lyf wt many thyng ordened ye parlement yf kynge henry durynge lyf went frome apoyntmente ony artycle cocludyd sayd parlemet sholde deposyd duke sholde take crowne kynge whyche thynges enacted thauctoryte whiche parlement ye comyns reame beynge assembled comyn hous comynyng treatyng vppon tytle sayd duke yorke sodeynly fell downe crowne whiche henge thenne myddes sayd hous whiche frayter abbaye westmynster whiche taken prodyce token regne ky ge henry endyd also crowne whiche stode hyghest toure stleple castell douer fell downe yere phow yorke slayne felde wakefelde ye seconde iourneye saynt albons ye quene prynce bicause quene prynce sone northe absent fro kynge obeyed suche thynges cocluded parlemente ordeyned duke yorke protector sholde go northwarde bryn quene subdue suche wolde obey whome went erle salysbury syr thomas neuyll sone moche people wakefelde norwaye ben loue pea afmarchaundyse dwelled see sydes assente irysshmen alwaye ydle poules knyghtes wayes buylded thre cytees deuelyn waterforde lymeryche encreaced rehell ayenste men lende brought fyrste sparthes irlonde fro turgesi tyme vnto roderyks tyme kynge connacia laste kynge londe xvii kynges irlonde kynges regned irlonde fro hermons tyme vnto laste roderyks tyme clxxxi kynges crowned neyther enoynted ne lawe herytage myght may strye strength armes seconde henry kynge englonde made roderyk subget yere kynge hentyes age xl regne xviii yere lorde xi hondred lxxii condidions maners irlonde ca xxvii solinus sayth men lo de ben straunge nacon houseles grete fyghters acout tyght wronge one thynge ben syngle clothynge scarse mete cruell herte angry speche drynketh fyrst blood dede men ben slayne wesshen theyr vysages therwith holde payd flesshe fruyt stede mete mylke stede drynke vsen moche playen yolenes huntynge trauayll lytell theyr chyldhode ben harde nourysshed harde fed vnsemely maners clothynge haue breche hosen allone wolle strayte hodes stretcheth cubyte ouer sholders behynde foldynges stede mantel clokes also sadels bootes ne spore whan de dryue theyr horse bred yerde ouer ende stede byte trench brydels reest vse brydeis letce hors etc theyr mete fyght ona med naked body netheles twoo dartes speres brode sparthes fyght one honde men forsaken tyllynge ldde keyen pasture bestes vse longe berdes longe locke hangynge downe behynde h de vse crafte flaxe wolle metall ne marchaudyse gyue hem ydelnes slouth reken rest lykynge fredome kyches thoughe scotlonde doughter irlonde vse harpe tymbire tabour netheles irysshmen connynge two manere instrumentes musyke harpe tymber armed wyre strenges bias whiche instrumentes though play hastely swyfeely make tygher merye armonye weladye thyche tewnes werbles note begynne bemoll playen secretly vnder dyme sowne greate strenges torne ayen vnto greetest partye crafte hydeth craft wolde seme though crafte hydde sholde ashamed yf take men ben euyll maners lyuynge paye tythynges wedde lawfully spare theyr alyes brother wedde brother wyfe ben besye betray neyghbours bere sperthes hondes stede staues fyght ayenst truste moost men ben varyable vnstedfaste trechours gylefull dealeth nedethe ware gyle crafte pea brennynge brondes hony tha galle malyce tha kuyghthode haue suche maners ben stronge warre batayle ne trewe pea become gossybs wyll falsly traye gossybrede holy kynred eueryche drynketh others bloode wha shedde loue somdele hir nouryce playfers whiche souke mylke souked whyle chyldren purse wher brethern theyr cosyns theyr othere kyn despysen theyr kyn whyles lyue auenge theyr deth whan ben slayne soo longe hath vsage euyll custome endured amonge hath goten maystrye ouer torneth treason kynde ferforthe ben traytours nature alyens men straunge londes dwelle amonge foloynge theyr maners vnneth none besmetted theyr treason also amo ge many men pyssen syttynge wymmen standynge ben many men lode foule shapen lymes body theyr lymmes lacke benefyce kynde soo noo ben none better shapen ben well shapen none worse shapen ben euyll shapen skylfully nature hurte defouled wyckednes lyuynge bryngethe suche foule gromes euyll shapen hem vnlawfull delynge foule maners euyll lyuynge wyckedly defouled kynde nature thys londe wale olde wyues wy men wonte ben yet men saye ofte scape themselfe lykenes hare mylke theyr neyghbours kyne stele mylke ofte grey houndes rennen pursewen wenen hare also craft nygromacye maken fatte swyne reed colour selle markettes fayres sone swyne passe onye water torne theyr owne kynde whether strawe heye gras turues swyne maye kepte craft tendure lykenes swyne ouer thre dayes amonge wondres take hede vttermest ende worlde falleth newe meruaylles wondres though ky de playde large loue secretlye ferre thendes openly nygh myddell therfore ylonde many gryselye wondres meruaylles pof meruaylles wondres irlonde ca xxviii many men tellen north syde irlonde londe lyfe ylond noman may deye whan ben olde vexed grete fekenes ben born nexte lond deye ther ylonde irlode woman therin may bere chylde yet may conceyue also ther ylonde whiche dede body maye roten vltonia vlster ylonde lake wonderly departed tweyne one parte grete dysturbaunce dyscomforth fendes partye gretely kynge comforth holy angel ther also saynt patryks purgatory yt shewed prayer coferme prechynge lore whan preched mysbyleued men sorowe payne euyll men sholde suffre euyl werkes ioy blysse gode men shall resceyue holy dedes telleth suffreth paynes purgatory yf enioyned hym penauce shall neuer suffre paynes hell deye fynally without repentaunce synne ensample sette full chapytre ende ptreuisa truly noman maye saued yf repentaut someuer penaunce euery repentaunt lyues ende shall sekerly saued though ueuer saynt patryks purgatorye ylonde conacte sale se conaccia halowed saynt brandon hath myse dede bodyes ben buryed ben kept erthe roten mamonia well wassheth hym wt water welle shall waxe hore heed wel vltonia soeuer wasshen therin shall neuer wexe hore afterwarde welle mounstre mamonia yf ony man touche welle none shall falle grete rayne prouynce rayne shall neuer cessetyll preste clene mayden synge masse chapelle faste blesse water mylke cowe one heer bespryngr welle reconcyle welle strauge manere glyndalcan thee saynt keyyn wythes betyth apple apple tree ben belsome sa ry holy saynt ough forth apple pia yers hele chylde seke lake vlster moche fyssh therin whiche xxx myle lengthe xv brede ryuer ban tennethe lake north occean men saye lake beganne maner men cou tree euyll lyuynge coeutes cu brutis well londe grete reuerence olde tyme alway couered yf lefte vncouered welle wolde ryse drowne londe happed woman wente well fetche water hyed fast chylde wepte cradell left well vncouered thenne well sprange fa drowned woman chyld made countre lake fysshe ponde preue grete argument whanne weder clere fysshers water se grounde vnder water roude toures hygh shapen steples chirches londe north syde irlonde countre ossyryens euery vii yere prayer holy abbot tweyne ben wedded man woman muste nedes eryled forshapen lyknes wolues abyde vii yere ende vii yere yf lyue come home gayne take agayne theyr owne shappe shall tweyne go forth theyr stede forshapen vii yere ther lake londe yf poole tree pyght stycked therin parte shafte poole erthe shall torne yron parte bydeth water shall come stone parte abydeth aboue shall tree owne kynde also ther lake tornethe basell asshe asshe hasell yf done therein also ikonde thre samon lrpes samons lepe ayemst tothe longe speres lenthe also leginia pounde seen colmans byrdes herdes ben called certelles come homely mannes honde yf men hem wro ge harme gone away come notte agayne water shall bytter stynke dydde wronge shall without wretche myschyef yf amendes pr touchynge patryks purgatorye ye shall vnderstonde seconde saynt patryk abbot bysshoppe whyle prechyd irlonde laboured studyed torne thylke wycked men lyued bestes euyll lyfe drede paynes helle conferme hem good lyfe sayd wolde orne theym myght know somwhat grete paynes also blysse spake thenne saynt patryk prayed god al myghty therfore lorde ihesu crist appyered saynt patryk toke hy staffe ladde hym wylde place shewed hym rounde pytte derke within sayd yf man repentaunt stable byleue wente pytte walkede therin daye nyght sholde se sorowes paynes euyll men ioy blysse good men thenne cryste vanysshed oute patryks syght saynt patryk red buylded chirche put therin chanons reguler closed pyt walle nowe chirche yerde atte eest ende chyrche faste shytte stronge doore man sholde nycely go without leue bysshoppe pryour place many men went com agayne patryks tyme tolde paynes ioy seen meruaylles sawe yette wryten cause therof many men torned conuerted ryght leue also many men wente come neuer agayne kynge stepneus kynge englande knyght swayne went saye come agayne swelled euer durynge lyfe p de ludensis ch dre chyste tolde many wonder hadde seen patryks per gatorye place called patryks purgatorye chyrche named reglis noman enioyned go purgatorye couseylled shold come therin take vpon hy penauce yf haue au rd stale wyll nedes go therin shall fyrste go bysshopp shall sente wich letter pryour place shall coutseyll hym leue yf wyll nedes goo therto shall prayer fastynge xv dayes xv dayes shal houseld ladde dore purgatorye process et ay yet shall couscylled le yf stedefaste wyll entre dore shall opened blessed go goddes name holde forth waye dore shall faste shette tyll nexte daye whan tyme pryour shall come opene dore yf man comen ledeth hym chirche processyon shall xv dayes prayer fastynge pof meruaylles sayntes irlonde ca xxix nere giraldus maketh mynde men nacyon ben angry men hasty take wretche whyles ben alyue sayntes halowes londe ben wretchefull sayntes othere londes clerkes londe ben chaste sayen many prayer done greate abstynence daye drynketh nyght aco ed myracle lechery regneth wyne regneth ben chosen abbayes clergye doone monkes sholde ben euyll ben worsto fall good men amonge theym choughe ben fewe good best prelate countre ben full slowe correccyon trespas besy contemplacyon prechynge goddes worde therfore sayntes londe ben confessours martyr amonge wonder prelate londe clerkes prelate sholde vnknowen therfore whan put ayenst bysshop cassyll myght many sayntes ben isio de neuer martyr amonge sythen men ben shrewed angry prelate sorycheles slowe correccons trespas bysshop answered frowardly ynoughe sayd oure men benshrewed angry inought themselfe goddes seruautes leye neuer honde hem greate reuerence worshyp englysshmen come londe make martyr wonte vse craft pr bysshop sayd bycause kynge henry leconde tho newe comen irlonde fresshly martyrdome sayt thomas caunterbury gir londe wale scotlonde ben belle staues croked hedes suche thynges relyques grete reuerence worshyp soo men londe dreden swere vp one thylpe belle golde staues vpon gospell ye chyef suche relyques holden thus staffe deuelyn whiche staff saye fyrste saynt patryk drofe wormes irlonde aug de ci dei ca vii yf menlaxe howe may dyuerse maner beestes dyuerse kynde kyndly goten bytwene mayl female come ben ylondes nots flode men supposen bestes swamme ylondes fyrste nexte forth othere el men sayllynge ylondes brought hem suche bestes loue hu tynge angel god almyghtyes co maundement brought suche beestes ylondes erthe brought forth fyrste fulfylled tho goddes co maundement commaunded erthe brynge forth gras quyche bestes phere endeth descrypcyon brytayne whiche conteyneth englonde wale scotlonde also bycause irlonde vnder rule englynde olde tyme hathe contynued therfore haue sette descrypcyon sayd beytayne whiche haue taken polycronycon bycause necessary engglysshmen know propretees comedytees meruaylles
